Leur cologie montre que la rserve peut tre caractrise comme msotrophe avec une tendance vers l'eutrophisation dans son ancien centre, et comme oligotrophe dans sa partie mridionale. La flore diatomique des eaux alimentant la rserve est domine par des espces des eaux msotrophes  eutrophes. Dans la rserve, la distribution des diatomes est surtout influence par le pH des eaux, de sorte que des espces rputes caractristiques des milieux oligo-  msotrophes ont t trouves, au lieu d'espces mso-  eutrophes, dans des tangs riches en nutriments, mais acides. During the period August 1978 - June 1979, we attempted to make an evaluation of water quality at about 20 sampling stations in the fen area of "De Zegge", by using an index based on the benthic diatoms. For this purpose 200 taxa, distributed over 27 genera were identified and categorised. Their ecology shows that the area is characterized as mesotrophic, with a tendency to eutrophication in its old centre and as oligotrophic in the south of the reserve. The diatom flora of the inflowing water is dominated by species of mesotrophic to eutrophic waters. Within the reserve, the distribution of diatoms is mainly influenced by the pH of the waters, in such a manner that species generally considered as characteristic of oligo- to mesotrophic waters were found instead of meso- to eutrophic species in points that are rich in nutrients but acidic.
20793964|La vgtation bryophytique terricole des talus argilo-limoneux a fait l'objet d'observations phytosociologiques et cologiques au Plateau des Tailles (Haute Ardenne belge). 20794075|Phosphatase activity (demonstrated by the lead trapping method) occurs mainly in the plasmalemma, mitochondria and tonoplast of maize roots (Zea mays L cv Anjou 18) and is Mg dependent. 20793586|Les interactions entre la forme d'azote (nitrate ou ammonium) et trois autres composantes du milieu alimentaire (le pH, les anions et les cations complmentaires) ont t tudies chez l'orge. L'absorption ionique est due, aussi bien en nutrition nitrique qu'ammoniacale,  l'action simultane de plusieurs types de mcanismes (diffusion, co-transport, pompe lectrognique). L'alimentation nitrique se caractrise par une absorption quilibre (la somme des cations absorbs est quivalente  celle des anions) et une translocation rapide des lments absorbs. L'absorption de l'anion nitrique est en bonne partie compense par celle du cation potassium. L'alimentation ammoniacale est, au contraire, dsquilibre (la somme des cations alimentaires est nettement suprieure  celles des anions, suite  la forte absorption d'ammonium), l'absorption potassique est faible et la translocation de certains ions est lente. The interaction between the nitrogen-source (nitrate or ammonium) and three other components of the nutrient solutions (pH, complementary anions and cations) has been studied or barley seedlings. The absorption of ions cannot be attributed to a single mechanism, but rather to the simultaneous functioning of several mechanisms (diffusion, co- and counter-transport). Nitrate-nutrition is characterized by a  balanced  absorption, a rather strong potassium-uptake and a fast translocation of the absorbed ions. Ammonium-nutrition, on the contrary, is characterized by an  unbalanced  absorption, a weak potassium-uptake and a poor translocation of some ions.

20793592|During 1972, microclimates have been compared in three ecosystems: a beech forest (130 years old), a planted spruce forest (55 years old) and a wet grassland (Filipendula ulmaria, Polygonum bistorta). The reference station is situated 3 km from the beech forest, in a grazed grassland at Smuid. The mean annual air temperature in beech and spruce forest is higher than the mean annual air temperature in the reference grassland. The difference in the air temperature between the beech and the spruce forest are very low (the maximum difference rarely exceed 1 C). The air temperature in the wet grassland is 1 to 4 C lower than in the reference grassland (especialy during july to december). During 1972, the variation of soil temperature at different levels in beech and spruce forest follows the same trends. The maximum temperatures are higher and the minimum temperatures are lower in the spruce forest than in the beech forest.

20793509|The annual biological cycle of lead has been studied comparatively in a Beech wood (Fagetum nudum, fig. 1) and in a Spruce plantation (Piceetum, fig. 2) growing on the same soil. The annual absorption of lead (tabl. 4) depends mainly on the primary productivity and phytochemical specifity of the ecosystem. The Piceetum is more productive and richer in lead (mainly in the bark of branches and in twigs, tabl. 2 and 3) than the Fagetum. Therefore, the annual absorption of lead in the former is much higher (312 g/ha) than in the latter (144 g/ha). Lead is highly accumulated in litter and decomposing organic matter (tabl. 5). The total quantities of lead accumulated in standing crop (aerial part) is nearly the same in the two forests, but the distribution among stems, branches and twigs is different (tabl. 2 and 3).

20792633|Lens culinaris has been shown to be long-day requiring for flowering. p-Hydroxybenzoc acid (p-HBA) stimulates growth and production of leaves of the mean stem of Lens both in short (10 hours) and long (16 hours) days. Chlorogenic acid (CA) stimulates growth in short days but has the inverse effect in long days. p-HBA and CA enhance flowering in short days, they delay it in long days. These results illustrate independence of growth and flowering towards phenolic compounds. They are in accord with the observations of Konishi and Galston (1964) and Zucker, Nitsch and Nitsch (1965) which concern the variations in the phenolic level in the leaves during floral induction and initiation: rise preceding changes at the meristem, drop during the differentiation of the flower primordia.

20792472|La teneur d'une plante en chacun des six lments majeurs se compose de deux parties: l'une est proportionnelle  la concentration de l'lment considr dans le milieu (action primaire), l'autre se compose d'une somme de termes, chacuns proportionnels  la concentration centsimale d'un des composants minraux dans le milieu (interaction). Un systme de sept quations du premier degr peut tre rsolu et donne, si la composition minrale de la plante entire est connue, la composition minrale et la dose de la solution utilise par la plante, ce que nous appelons  richesse utile  dans le cas d'un sol non additionn d'engrais. Inversment, connaissant la composition d'une solution minrale, il est possible de dterminer approximativement la composition minrale de la plante ceci particulirement dans le cas du cotonnier. The percentage of the dry matter for each of the six major elements can be considered as composed of two parts: one is proportional to the concentration of the considerate element in the medium (primary action), the other one is composed of a sum of terms each proportional to the percentage of the concentration in the medium of one of the mineral components (interaction). A set of seven equations of the first degree can so be solved and give, if the mineral composition of the whole plant is known, the mineral composition of the solution used by the plant (what we call  richesse utile  in the case of a soil without any addition of nutrients). Inversely, knowing the composition of a mineral solution, it is possible to determine approximately the mineral composition of the plant, this in the particular case of cottonbush.

20792849|La 5-fluorodsoxyuridine (FUdR) est rpute inhiber spcifiquement la synthse du DNA. Cette substance devrait, par consquent, inhiber les divisions cellulaires. Appliqu au mristme caulinaire de Sinapis, le FUdR diminue fortement l'activit mitotique. Cette dernire peut tre rtablie par un traitement  la thymidine, un antidote du FUdR. Ces rsultats sont conformes aux prvisions mais d'autres observations montrent que le FUdR peut empcher la division de cellules ayant termin la duplication de leur DNA (cellules se trouvant en phase G du cycle mitotique). L'action de cet inhibiteur sur les cellules mristmatiques est donc de nature complexe. Effect of 5-fluorodeoxyuridine on the mitotic activity of the shoot apical meristem of Sinapis alba L.  5-fluorodeoxyuridine (FUdR) is known to be a specific inhibitor of DNA synthesis. Consequently this compound is expected to inhibit cell divisions. When applied on the shoot apical meristem of Sinapis, FUdR strongly decreased the mitotic activity. Its effect was overcome by adding thymidine, a specific precursor of DNA. These results are in agreement with the previsions, but other observations indicated that FUdR could prevent the division of cells having completed the duplication of their DNA, i. e. cells in the G-phase of the mitotic cycle. The effect of this inhibitor on the meristematic cells seems complex.

20793874|Un chantillon de gnotypes utiliss en Belgique a t tudi en milieu contrl. Les effets de la temprature, de la longueur du jour et de la photopriode ont t examins. En moyenne, une augmentation de la photopriode de 4 heures retarde d'une semaine l'apparition des soies. D'autre part, si photopriode et dure du jour sont allonges simultanment, les traitements sont sans effets. Le nombre de feuilles augmente avec la photopriode et la temprature tandis que la longueur des tiges est drastiquement rduite aux photopriodes les plus courtes. A sample of genotypes used in Belgium was studied in controlled environment. The effect of constant temperature (20 and 30C), daylength (duration of light with photon flux density of 20 nE/s/cm) and photoperiod (daylength plus lengthening with light at 1 nE/s/cm) were examined. On an average an increase of 4 hours in photoperiod delayed silking by one week. A simultaneous increase of photoperiod and daylength was without effect. Number of leaves increased with photoperiod and temperature and stem height was reduced drastically at the shorter photoperiods.

20793470|A set of experiments was performed in order to investigate the action of calcium on the absorption of potassium and sodium by excised barley roots (Hordeum distichum L. cultivar Mosane). It was shown that Calcium does not manifest the same effects wether applied in the culture solution or in the absorption phase. When applied in the culture solution, calcium always acts favorably on the subsequent absorption of K and Na. When applied in the absorption solutions, at concentrations ranging from 10 to 10 me Calcium/liter, calcium:  promotes the absorption of K  inhibits to a lesser extent the absorption of Na. Both effects should be explained by an action of calcium on a K-Na active pomp.
20792791|Aerial biomass and productivity of a copsewood (Orchimont-Belgium). Biomass and annual productivity of an oak and birch copsewood have been studied during 1968 at Orchimont (Semois-Belgium). Wood and leaves production of the shrubs from the four main species, Quercus robur (oak), Betula pendula (birch), Sorbus aucuparia (service-tree), and Corylus avellana (hazel), have been studied; herbaceous plants (Stellaria holostea, Viola riviniana, Holcus mollis, Pteridium aquilinum) have been considered all together. 20792684|The toxic and mutagenic activity of the isomeric forms (L, D and meso) of diepoxybutane has been investigated in Arabidopsis thaliana. In the treated generation, differences between isomers were found for various criteria: growth rate, survival at maturity, fertility and morphological abnormalities. The activity was decreasing from L to D to meso. The same response to the isomers occured in M generation for chlorophyll and morphological mutations. The percentages of mutations were: L = 7.2; D = 2.1 and meso = 1.0. As regards the frequencies of chlorophyll mutant types obtained, no difference between the 3 isomers was found. Possible interpretations of quantitative differences between isomers were proposed.

20792638|Taxonomic notes about the Haemodoraceae and the Hypoxidaceae (Monocotyledones). These families were often poorly defined and confused with the Amaryllidaceae. It seems they are good families, both characterized by a same and particular embryology but separate according to the floral and the foliar morphologies; the Haemodoraceae have folded-welded leaves and the Hypoxidaceae have not this character.

20792501|Perilla nankinensis (Lour.) Decne (a short day strain), grown in long days, was treated by phosfon-D (a growth retardant), gibberellic acid or both substances. Stem length and leaf area were strongly reduced by phosfon-D applied via the root system but the rate of leaf formation was not affected. The ability of cell division in subapical pith was lowered. No effect was observed upon mitotic activity of apical meristem itself. Gibberellic acid, applied via the apices and youngest leaves, stimulated the mitotic activity within the subapical pith and the peripheral zone of the shoot apex. These increases of the number of cell divisions were respectively linked to an enhancement of stem growth and an acceleration of the plastochronic functioning. Gibberellic acid applied on plants previously treated by phosfon-D completely overcame the reduction of stem length and inhibition of subapical mitotic activity caused by the growth-retardant. However, the activity of the peripheral zone of the apical meristem as well as the rate of leaf formation were not affected.

20793980|A series of FORTRAN-IV computer programs for the creation and the analysis of vegetation data is described. The central utility program, INQUIKIN, facilitates the entering, the checking and the analysis of the data. A fixed alphabetical reference list of taxa plays an important role in the set up of vegetation data banks. The central utility program enables the application of a variety of data analytical programs including ordination and classification methods. The implemented Cornell Ecology Programs constitute the major part of the data-analytical programs. Multivariate analysis and computers in general may be considered as important ancillaries in vegetation science. Although they provide a powerful tool for data analysis they may be abused in different ways. Een reeks FORTRAN-IV computer programma's voor de opbouw en de analyse van vegetatietabellen wordt besproken. De kern wordt gevormd door het programma INQUIKIN dat het invoeren, het controleren en de analyse van vegetatiegegevens vergemakkelijkt. Een alfabetische lijst van alle taxa speelt hierbij een belangrijke rol. Dit centrale programma sluit direkt aan op een brede waaier van verwerkingsprogramma's. De belangrijkste verwerkingsprogramma's behoren tot de "Cornell Ecology Programs". Tot slot wordt gewezen op een aantal gevaren die het gebruik van computers met zich meebrengt. Desondanks dienen numerieke methoden beschouwd te worden als belangrijke hulpmiddelen bij de analyse van gegevens uit de vegetatiekunde.
20793572|Samples of Lolium multiflorum Lam. var. italicum (A. Brann) G. Beck and Trifolium repens L. have been cultivated in vegetation pots and exposed during summer and early automn in several sites of the city (Brussels, fig. 1) and in the country (Smuid, High Belgium). 20793569|L'ion calcium donn en cours de culture ou en cours d'absorption exerce un effet sur l'absorption de K et de Na. L'utilisation du calcium en cours de culture est indispensable pour l'obtention de racines saines aux structures intactes et aux proprits d'absorption optimales. La prsence de calcium en cours d'absorption dtermine:  un effet positif immdiat et rversible sur l'absorption du potassium,  un effet ngatif immdiat et rversible, positif et rversible  plus long terme sur l'absorption du sodium. Ces rsultats sont expliqus sur la base d'un modle thorique qui, outre les phases classiques de libre diffusion, de Donnan et d'absorption active, tient compte de proprits de sorption propers au cytoplasme et influences par la prsence de calcium. The effect of calcium has been tested on the absorption of potassium and sodium by excised barley roots. Calcium has to be present in the culture solution to assure the production of excised roots with a good absorption capacity due to formation of normal membrane and cytoplasmic structures. When applied in absorption phase, together with the monovalent cations, Ca exerts:  a positive immediate and reversible effect on the absorption of K,  a negative effect of shorter duration on Na absorption, followed by a delayed activation of the absorption. Both effects are reversible. These results are explained on the basis of a theoretical model which postulates the existence of an important sorption phase in the cytoplasm.
20792769|A preliminary phytogeochemical study, based on polyelements, Na, C1 and Si foliar analysis, has been made on the riverain vegetation of the  ruisseau de Gembes  (Daverdisse, Ardennes). High N content of the studied alluvial soils and good nitrification conditions probably give account of N high level in the plants. On the other side, the very coarse texture and K poorness of the soils may be considered as responsable of the very bad K plant nutrition.

20792819|The mixed oak forest of Virelles (near Chimay, Belgium) is established on a limestone plateau. Formerly human action by clearing stones to allow shifting cultivation differentiated locally deeper soil ( brown calcareous soil ) from the originally rendsina (fig. 1 and 3). The soil types are briefly characterized and their extension mapped (fig. 2). The organic matter of both soils is studied by the method of Duchaufour and Jacquin. The humification is very different (tabl. 1 and 2). So, in the rendsina the fulvicshumics acids ratio is low and also the rate of humification (45%); the humus is a calcic Mull. The contrary happens in the  brown calcareous soil  where the rate of humification reaches 82% of the total carbon; the humus is like a Cryptomull.

20792823|K, Ca, Mg, N, S and P have been analysed in the leaves of dominant plant species of a coal mine at Chapelle-lez-Herlaimont, near Charleroi (Belgium). 20792729|Although many reports have been published concerning the production of excised barley roots having a high ability to take up salts, no standard growing medium have been used. The roots are mostly grown in liquid culture of CaSO solution. In this study, an attempt has been made to determine the influence of culture conditions on the subsequent absorption of sulfate. When barley roots are grown in liquid culture supplied with anions NO, SO, HPO and cations K, Ca and Mg, the consequent sulfate uptake is greatly affected. It is of great interest for all the workers using excised barley roots to uniformise their technical method, especially in regard to the production of roots in a standard nutrient medium.

20793862|In the Leiemeersen a clear zonation of marsh towards meadow vegetation, correlated with environmental conditions (groundwater-level) and past human interference (rising of the water table, neglect of management) can be observed. The vegetation has been studied using the Braun-Blanquet-approach, and analysed with some help of numerical methods. Actually the following vegetation types have been identified: a community of Phragmites australis, a community of Carex acutiformis and Filipendula ulmaria, a community of Phalaris arundinacea, and a meadow community with Caltha palustris. Their syntaxonomical position is discussed. It is pointed out that the classification within the traditional Braun-Blanquet-system is difficult because of the derelict character of the vegetation. The processes coupled with dereliction, namely changes in structure and composition of the vegetation, expansion and finally dominance of competitive species (mainly tall forbs), suppression of low-growing species (mainly meadow species) are discussed. Finally, some management rules for nature conservation purposes are given. In de Leiemeersen treedt een duidelijk zonatiepatroon van moeras- naar hooilandvegetaties op, dat zowel gecorreleerd is met milieufactoren (voornamelijk grondwaterniveau) als met de vroegere menselijke benvloeding (stijging van de watertafel, verwaarlozen van het beheer). De vegetatie werd bestudeerd via de Braun-Blanquet-methode; bij de analyse werden tevens numerieke technieken gebruikt. De volgende vegetatietypen worden onderscheiden: een Phragmites australis-vegetatie, een Carex acutiformis-Filipendula ulmaria-vegetatie, een Phalaris arundinacea-vegetatie, en een hooilandvegetatie met Caltha palustris. Hun syntaxonomische plaatsing wordt besproken. Het blijkt dat de classificatie binnen het traditionele Braun-Blanquet-systeem sterk wordt bemoeilijkt door het verruigde karakter van de vegetaties. De verruigingsprocessen die optreden bij verwaarlozen van het beheer worden besproken. Tenslotte worden enkele richtlijnen geformuleerd in verband met het te voeren natuurbeheer.

20792657|Both the potentials of the cytoplasm and the vacuole are simultaneously measured in the internodal cell of Nitella flexilis, dipped in solutions where rubidium is substituted for potassium (or sodium). Cells pretreated in Ca-free medium are used throughout the experiments. In the external solutions (KCl + NaCl, RbCl + NaCl, KCl + RbCl) the ratio of ions is varied but the total concentration kept constant at 2 mM. At the plasmalemma level, the results cannot be fitted to Goldman type equation containing the measured cytoplasmic concentrations in K and Na ions, without introducing variations of the permeability coefficients with external conditions and a contribution of Cl ions. The graphics suggest the following relations for these coefficients: PK  PRb  PNa (in the presence of K) and PRb  PNa (in the absence of K). At the tonoplast level, the potential difference between the vacuole and the cytoplasm is unaffected by concentration changes provided that K ions are present in external solutions (some exceptions are noted in relative large concentrations of rubidium). In K-free solutions, there is a increasing hyperpolarization of the vacuole with respect to the bathing medium and independent of the sign and the magnitude of the tonoplast potential. An electrically neutral active transport process is proposed. Total resistances determinations for the two membranes have shown an inverse relation with external Rb concentrations and confirmed in Nitella that the fluxes of rubidium are less than those of potassium.

20793464|Bien que fort semblables en microscopie optique et en microscopie lectronique  balayage, les spores de Mycenastrum et d'Abstoma se distinguent par la structure de la paroi, qui rapproche plus Mycenastrum des Scleroderma et, par certains aspects, Abstoma des Lycoperdon. 20793840|The status of hyperaccumulators (plants with heavy metal levels exceeding 1000 g/g in dried leaves) of copper and cobalt is reviewed and fresh data presented. Hyperaccumulators are confined exclusively to the Copper Belt of Zare/Zambia and number 15 cobaltophytes and 12 cuprophytes. Confinement of these taxa to the Copper Belt is presumed to be due to the large area of this metallogenic province compared with copper/cobalt occurrences elsewhere so that a multiplicity of metal-accumulating species have evolved in the course of time. Most of the hyperaccumulators belong to advanced families such as the Labiatae and Scrophulariaceae. La notion d'hyperaccumulateur (plante dont la teneur des feuilles sches en mtaux lourds dpasse 1000 g/g) de cuivre et de cobalt est revue et complte par des rsultats indits. La distribution de ces hyperaccumulateurs est entirement limite au Copperbelt zaro-zambien; leur nombre s'lve respectivement  15 cobaltophytes et 12 cuprophytes. L'endmisme de ces taxons dans le Copperbelt est suppos tre d  la grande superficie de cette province mtallognique en comparaison avec l'tendue des affleurements de cuivre et de cobalt observs ailleurs. C'est ainsi que s'est dvelopp, au cours du temps, un nombre considrable d'espces accumulatrices de mtaux lourds. La plupart des hyperaccumulateurs appartiennent  des familles volues, telles que les Labiatae et les Scrophulariaceae.

Distribution and ecology of H. armoricum are studied in the Ardennes massif. Known from 24 IFB-squares (16 km) before 1930, it is recorded today from 59 IFB-squares: 38 from the Stavelot cambro-ordovician massif, 18 from the Rocroi massif and 3 isolated localities. This species is almost restricted to acid-oligotrophic streams running through the Revinian, Devillian, Salmian and sometimes Gedinnian: acid waters (pH 4-6.5), low mineralisation (0.5-1.5 meq/l), low Ca content (<10 ppm), no or low alcalinity (<10 ppm CaCO) and high SO content (10-25 ppm). It is only known from one locality on Siegenian rocks and completely absent from Emsian regions. H. armoricum grows preferentially in woody shady places, on rocky or fine gravely banquettes along the streams as well as on rocks, wet places under overhanging banks and under small cascades. It forms a very characteristic community in the zone between low- and high-water level, between terricolous and aquatic bryophytes-communities. A compared phytosociological and ecological study in the Ardennes, Britanny and Cotentin will be dealt with in a further paper.

20792730|Monolayers of chlorophyll a were spread at a water-air interface in a Wilhelmy plate film balance, and surface isotherms were measured under various conditions. On aqueous phosphate buffer at pH = 7.8, the area/molecule (extrapolated to zero pressure) was 122 . Upon illumination in air, chlorophyll monolayers undergo photo-oxidation which results in a decrease of the film pressure when the pigment is oxidized. The quantum yield for this reaction when the monolayer is initially compressed to 17 dyne / cm is calculated to be 0.06. This is more than 10 times greater than the yield for photo-oxidation in a dilute solution of chlorophyll a in benzene. For expanded monolayers (initial pressure of 2 dyne / cm) the reaction is considerably less efficient than for the compressed monolayers, which suggests that energy transfer is important in the photochemistry of these monolayers. In mixed monolayers of chlorophyll and carotene, the photo-oxidation of chlorophyll is inhibited.

20792496|Seeds of Vicia faba, Nigella damascena and Hordeum sativum were treated with pure oleic acid for 2-24 hr and roots of Allium cepa with water emulsions of oleic acid in different proportions for 2 hr. 20793538|Various expressions of plant water content,  water content as a percentage of fresh weight or dry wheight, water saturation deficit (WSD) and relative turgidity (RT), hydratability (H),  are critically examined, chiefly as parameters of the water potential (WP), the latter being with much more difficulty measured. At this point of view, WSD (or RT) is widely used as parameter of WP, but relation WSD (or RT)/WP is specific and calibration is needed for any studied species. Hydratability (Homs, 1942), which clearly takes into account the ratio of dry matter, displays in terms of WSD a pattern which is similar to that one of the WP; further the relation H/WP is fairly independent with respect to the specific diversity; hydratability seems thereby a better parameter of the WP than WSD or RT. Dynamic aspects on leaf-litter disappearance.  1. The disappearance rate of leaves of Fagus sylvatica, Quercus robur, Carpinus betulus, Tilia platyphyllos, Acer campestre, A. pseudoplatanus, Fraxinus excelsior, Prunus avium and Corylus avellana is studied in three stations of the mixed calcareous oak-forest at Virelles (Belgium). Soil profiles are either of the superficial stony type or more or less deeply cleared. 2. The sequence of morphological aspects of the litter is typified by five steps of decay based on losses of leaf area. 3. Breakdown rates are specific and related to the C/N ratios of the leaves. Leaves of Carpinus, Tilia, Fraxinus, Prunus, Corylus with a C/N ratio lower than 30 disappear within seven months; leaves of Quercus and Fagus with a C/N ratio higher than 40 decompose more slowly (twelve and fifteen months respectively). Leaves of Acer with an intermediate C/N ratio disappear within eight or nine months. 4. Decay of Quercus and Fagus leaves is more effective where the soil is deeply cleared of stones. 5. The breakdown rates of the different leaf sorts enable us to know the specific composition of the litter and to compute the evolution of its biomass during the year. 6. Celluloytic and ligninolytic activities of the soils, as well as decay rates of Quercus and Fagus leaves, are higher in the soils deeply cleared of stones. 7. The quick turn-over of the litter undergoes dynamic variations which are related on the one hand, to qualitative and quantitative differences in the ligneous populations and on the other hand, to the more or less man-modified types of soils.

20792851|Evapotranspiration of the epiphytic vegetation overgrowing the lower part of oak (Quercus robur) and mapple-tree (Acer campestre) trunks in the mixed oak forest at Virelles-Blaimont.  In the mixed oak forest at Virelles-Blaimont, the biomass of epiphytic layer overgrowing the bark at the lower part of the trunks (between 0 and 1 m) of Quercus robur and Acer campestre amounts 355, 1 kg/ha in early year 1970. Its water saturation capacity, reached with a 8,0 mm rainfall during the leafy phenophase, is estimated at 0,133 mm. During this period, the water content of epiphytes (We) is linked with the atmospheric evaporating power (Ep = Piche) by the following relation: $\text{W}_{\text{e}}=0,1542\ \text{E}_{\text{p}}^{-0,64}$ With the number, the size and the periodicity of showers, one can estimate, using this relation, the water content of epiphytic layer before and after each rain and obtain by subtraction the evapotranspiration between two successive showers. The calculations show that the mean evapotranspiration by shower is equal to 0,059 mm. Extrapolation to the whole leafy phenophase (mean of three periods: 1966, 1967 and 1968), the epiphytic vegetation of the lower part of the trunks may be assumed to evapotranspirate about 5,0 mm (0.92% of the total rainfall or 1,18% of the phytocenose evapotranspiration). This work shows that, in the studied ecosystem, there is a slight overestimation of the infiltration water by omitting the evapotranspiration of the epiphytic vegetation overgrowing the trunks under the run-off channels.

20792499|Auxin-oxidasic activity, peroxidase, catalase and phenoloxidase have been comparatively studied in extracts from beans' roots and hypocotyls cultivated in the dark or in the light. Furthermore, the effectors' capacity of these extracts has been investigated  after boiling  on the activity of purified peroxidase, catalase and phenoloxidase, in their own property and in their respective capacity to oxidize IAA. Beans' extracts show IAA-oxidase, peroxidase and catalase but not phenoloxidase; they also contain effectors of peroxidase and catalase, respectively in their property to oxidize phenols and to decompose hydrogen peroxide and in their property to destroy IAA too. No trace of phenoloxidasic effectors is detected so that phenol-oxidase does not seem to be present. Auxin-oxidasic activity is diminished when Phaseolus is cultivated in the light: cinetic curves indicate that this diminution is due to a light induced increase in natural inhibitors of the enzymic auxin degradation. Because the extracts from the light cultivated beans are more inhibitory of the auxin catabolism by a purified peroxidase (horseradish) and by a purified catalase (bovin liver) than extracts from the dark cultivated ones, it is concluded that peroxidase and catalase at least participate to auxin destruction by Phaseolus extracts. Purified tyrosinase (mushroom) does not catalyse IAA destruction. The copper nature of the enzymic IAA degradation proposed by Wagenknecht et Burris (1950) is discussed. Light not only modifies the effectors metabolism of peroxidase and catalase when they attack IAA but also when they oxidize phenols or decompose hydrogen peroxide. Phenols and hydrogen peroxide have an important action in auxin degradation. Thus there is possibility of a new pathway of the light action on auxin catabolism in vivo.

20792476|1. Male and female thalli of Marchantia polymorpha L. were grown separately, in ashes in a very shaded greenhouse, under 8-hour photoperiods of white fluorescent light (with diffuse natural light). If mutual overgrowing of the thalli was avoided by transplanting the young parts ( 3 cm long) in due time, homogenous cultures were obtained. Under these conditions, Marchantia remained vegetative, but we noticed a clearcut dimorphism: the male thalli had more gemmae-cups than the female; their lobes were not as broad and their growth was not as horizontal as that of the female thalli. Comparable differences between vegetative plants had been observed by Voth (1941). Exclusively under white light, in a dark-room, we noticed the same dimorphism. 2. Experiments were done in two dark-rooms, studying the influence of short farred irradiations at the end of daily periods of white fluorescent light, in 24-hour light-dark cycles. Five minutes, even 1 minute of far-red, given at the end of each 8-hour photoperiod, causes a strong orthotropism and a very different morphology. Already after the first cycle (only after one far-red exposure), the margins of the young parts are curled upwards in both male and female thalli; if the treatment is continued, the effects become very strong, and after one month, the far-red treated thalli, male as well as female, differ enormously from the controls by their orthotropic ramifications, much narrower lobes, different shape and different colour. With a daily sequence of alternate far-red and red exposures at the end of the photoperiod, there is always complete reversibility of the action of the preceding one by the following one; the thalli receiving 2 1/2 min red after 5 min far-red were of the same outlook as the controls. 3. This repeated reversibility and the strong effect of rather short irradiations suggest the presence in the thalli of Marchantia of the same photoreversible pigment, phytochrome, as known in higher plants. 4. We emphasize the similarity of our results on the vegetative growth of Marchantia with those of Downs et al. (1957) on the elongation of internodes in Phaseolus vulgaris L.; in both species, the effect of a given far-red exposure is stronger at the end of short days than at the end of long days. 5. Our present working hypothesis is that the presence of the P form of phytochrome inhibits the upward bending (orthotropic growth) and the narrowing of the lobes; the conversion by far-red light of the pigment in the P form which is believed to be physiologically inactive (Borthwick & Hendricks, 1961), allows orthotropic growth and the formation of long, narrow lobes. According to this viewpoint, the orthotropism and the etiolation should be stronger the longer the pigment is kept in the P form during each 24-hour period. We have indeed found (Frederciq, 1964, and present publication) that the action of 5 minutes far-red is much stronger after 8-hour photoperiods (P form present only during 8 hours per 24 hours) than after 16-hour days (P form present during 16 hours per 24 hours). 6. Ten minutes far-red have a stronger effect immediately at the end of an 8-hour day, than in the middle of the 16-hour night. The fact that 5 minutes far-red causes a marked orthotropism and changement in morphology even when applied in the middle of the 16-hour night, indicates that the % of P present at that moment still prevents orthotropism and etiolation. In the middle of the 16-hour nights, as at the end of the 8-hour days, or at the end of the 16-hour days, there is the same complete reversibility of the far-red effect by 2 1/2 minutes red light. 7. Five, even 1 minute of far-red light at the end of 16-hour photoperiods cause a marked orthotropism, while the thalli receiving 1 hour of light + 23 hours of darkness remain nearly flat. This suggests that a not very high % of P is sufficient to keep the thalli growing horizontally, or that the disappearance of P (reversion or destruction) is slow. Under 8- or 16-hour photoperiods of incandescent light, the thalli also bend upwards, although not as strongly as with terminal far-red exposures; this makes the second alternative (slow disappearance of P) more probable. 8. The action of a far-red irradiation is not as great after 1-hour photoperiods as after 4- or 8-hour ones; this is not in contradiction with our hypothesis (no 5), if it is assumed that substrate is limiting, and we observed that the controls scarcely grew with only one hour of light per day. Downs et al. (1957) also noticed in Phaseolus a weaker elongating effect, if far-red was applied after 1- or 2- hour photoperiods than after 4- or 6- hour ones. Ninnemann & Halbsguth (1965) have shown that also the growth of gemmalings of Marchantia is controlled by the phytochrome system. 9. With Lunularia cruciata L. and Conocephalum conicum (L.) Dum., we observed the same photoreversibility, but the effects of far-red light are not as great as in Marchantia. Wilson & Schwabe (1964) working on a palestinian variety of Lunularia cruciata, showed that the dormancy and resumption of growth are phytochrome mediated. 10. With Dr. De Greef, we found lower chlorophyll a and b levels in the far-red treated thalli than in the controls; this depressive effect was reversed by red light; these results are published elsewhere. 11. The factors determining the formation of gemmae-cups are complex, and our first published results as preliminary observations in 1964, will be studied in more depth.

20792502|Auxin-oxidasic effectors from Zea Mays green leaves have been extracted and separated by thin layer chromatography. All the effectors are negative (inhibitors). 20794087|Copper, cobalt and 16 other elements were determined in 838 specimens of plants growing over the copper/cobalt deposits of Central Africa in Zambia and Shaba Region, Zare. The work resulted in the identification of a further nine hyperaccumulators (> 1000 g/g in dry plant material) of cobalt and eleven of copper, with a further three taxa hyperaccumulating both elements. Statistical analysis of the data showed that the copper and cobalt levels in plant material correlated with each other and with iron. Accumulation of these three elements was presumed to be due to the ability of certain plants to form organometallic complexes with many transition elements. Relative uptake of cobalt was greater than that of copper due to the tendency of most plants to restrict inordinate uptake of plant nutrients. Factor analysis of the data showed that 60% of the variance of the system (i.e. elemental concentrations) was accounted for by aluminium, boron, calcium, cobalt and copper. Principal components analysis showed that the concentration data could be reduced to seven factors (accounting for 71.3% of the variance), two of which were strongly influenced by copper and cobalt. 20792697|During the year 1968, soil respiration was measured by the Walter-Haber's inverted box method in a mixed oak-forest at Virelles (Belgium). Results are correlated with soil temperature and moisture. Ammoniacal and nitric nitrogen contents in the humic layer were monthly determined and mineralization in situ and in vitro examined continuously. Mineral nitrogen content is low, especially for nitrates. Incubation in situ gives annual net mineralization which is about 100 mg for 100 g organic matter and is for the main part the result of an important nitrification process. Mineralization in the drying-room gives systematically higher values. The evolution of morphological aspects of the litter has been studied; five steps of decay based on losses of leave surfaces are described. Rate of decomposition of Quercus robur and Fagus sylvatica leaves has been experimentally checked in situ. Oak-leaves disappear in 12 months, most of the beech-leaves in 15 months. Cellulolytic and ligninolytic activities have been estimated by simple methods.

20793842|L'analyse des biochromatogrammes, durant l'enracinement, montre qu'au moins deux substances, C et IAA like-substance, semblent tre impliques dans la formation des racines de Zebrina. La quantit de ces substances augmente dans le nud au dbut de la rhizognse. La substance C ne se trouve jamais dans l'entre-nud o aucune racine ne se forme. The rooting test confirms the initiation power for root development of the two substances.
20792725|Some environmental factors of the Belgian Plagiotheciaceae are investigated. This study suggests that the chemical nature of the substratum (pH, Ca, carbon-nitrogen ratio) is of some importance in the ecological requirements of the Plagiotheciaceae. Three groups of species are recognized on the basis of these observations. The first one with I. wissgrillii, basiphil and calcicolous taxon. The second with I. elegans, P. laetum, P. curvifolium, P. denticulatum and P. undulatum, acidiphil species on low mineralized substratum. The third group with 3 closely related species, P. sylvaticum, P. succulentum and P. roeseanum, neutrophil taxa on higher mineralized substratum. The amplitude of the variations of these factors is also measured and provides some informations on the degree of adaptability of the taxa. P. denticulatum, P. succulentum, P. laetum and I. elegans are the most tolerant species and have a large geographical distribution in Belgium.

20794123|Sphaerocarpos michelii, no more observed in Belgium since 1880, has recently been rediscovered at three places. The range of the tetrad diameter of S. michelii given in the literature (75-120 m) is not correct. The mean tetrad diameter of the eleven collections of S. michelii studied is 125 m (extremes: 80-170 m), and of eight Belgian collections of S. texanus, 144 m (extremes: 105-190 m). Tetrad diameter is not a valuable diagnostic character to distinguish S. michelii from S. texanus. Many collections of S. michelii have spores with a median papilla in the areoles. This character is absent in the S. texanus collections studied. The Belgian distribution of S. michelii is given and its habitat is described. Sphaerocarpos michelii Bellardi en Belgique. Setaria splendida, of the tribe Paniceae, originates from the South of Central Africa and is well appreciated in tropical herbages at high altitude. It is usually established vegetatively as germination is poor. Percentage of full spikelets is low and rises up to 31%. Germination of spikelets is low foor seeds aged 7 months, it improves with age and 23% is obtained for seeds 15 months old. The following treatments: dehulling, chilling, boric acid, gibberellic acid, hydrogen peroxyde, heat, do not improve so much germination rate. Cycles of wetting and drying enhance germination and give a 41% rate.

20792727|Membrane potentials and electrical resistances of Nitella flexilis (L) Ag. are measured at 3 and 19C as functions of external KCl + NaCl concentrations and time. Cells pretreated in Ca-free medium are used troughout the experiments. In 1,9 mM NaCl + 0,1 mM KCl solution a depolarization and a large increasing (during about one hour) rectification are observed when the cell is stored at 3C. When the temperature is normal, no such phenomena can be recorded. When Nitella cells are dipped during two hours in this solution at 3C the variation of the p.d. by changing the external medium to 0,1 mM NaCl + 1,9 mM KCl is half lesser than it would be by such a change for a not treated cell at normal temperature. From all these results it is concluded that when ionic pumps are inhibited by the cold, the predominance of Na on K in external medium increases the permeability of the membrane to Na ions and induces a paired efflux of potassium and chloride. In 0,1 mM NaCl + 1,9 KCl solution, whatever the temperature, a very small hyperpolarization and an inverse of the former rectification are observed during the storing of the cells. It is assumed that an influx of Cl and K is induced by predominance of external K ions. As the 3C resistance / 19C resistance ratio of the cell remains constant whatever the external solution, it is concluded that it is more the ionic environment than the cooling which induces the observed differential modifications of the membrane conductance. Therefore it is postulated that the specificity of the membrane depends primarily upon an adsorption process which induces secondarily a modification of the passive diffusion of the mobile ions.

20793596|The particular conditions of the Woluwe river, one of the last still flowing through the eastern part of Brussels, were analysed. 20793853|Pellia borealis Lorbeer est un autodiplode de P. epiphylla (L.) Corda. L'tude des colonies de thalles rcolts dans 17 stations belges choisies dans une large gamme d'altitudes a port sur le nombre chromosomique, la taille des cellules marginales du thalle, les dimensions des spores et des cellules de la paroi externe de la capsule. A taxonomical study of Pellia borealis Lorbeer which is an autodiploid of P. epiphylla (L.) Corda was carried out. Thalli were collected in 17 Belgian localities, at various altitudes. For each sample, the chromosome number was determined; moreover, marginal cells of thalli, capsule wall cells and spores were measured. It becomes apparent that P. borealis can only be distinguished from P. epiphylla by the characters of the sporophyte. It is restricted to high altitudes of the Ardennes and appears to be a real boreal-mountain liverwort. It is concluded that P. borealis should be regarded as a subspecies of P. epiphylla: Pellia epiphylla (L.) Corda subsp. borealis (Lorbeer) V. Messe, comb. nov.

20793924|A number of physical and chemical data regarding the soil and the surface water of the peat-bog 'Buitengoor-Meergoor' (Mol, Belgium) are discussed. A description is given of the spatial variation in these abiotic factors. This variation consists mainly of changes in water-level, ion concentration and pH, which are in turn predominantly controlled by the relief. In broad outline the pH of the surface water ranges from about 7 in the part of the area influenced by ion rich seepage to about 3 on the drier and rather ombrotrophic places, which surround the lower lying seepage area. The total ion concentration varies accordingly between about 12 meq/l and 2 meq/l. 20793571|Ruderal vegetation on wasted soils in the Eastern zone of the Brussels ecosystem has been studied, concerning their structure, biomass, productivity and mineralomass. Specially two types of phytogeocenoses, the Tanaceto-Artemisietum vulgaris and the Solidaginetum giganteae, having a phytomass of more than 20 t/ha, have been studied. Their very high productivity (14-20 t/ha/year) is obtained using a mineral cycling where potassium (K) and not nitrogen (N) is the dominating element.

20794086|At the Luiswishi site, in the surroundings of Lubumbashi (Zare), on a red ochre zonal soil, three vegetation types are found, belonging to the same succession. Soil moisture was followed during a 15-months period. Comparison of soil water reserves indicated that the substitution of the dry evergreen forest, the ecosystem frequently admitted to be the climax of Upper Shaba, by the woodland produces a clear decrease (64 mm or 5.0% of the mean annual rainfall) for the upper two metres. Moreover this modification is reinforced by the reduction of Macrotermes activity, inducing a greater number of abandoned termitaria, a more xeric milieu. Protection of soil by the forest canopy thus appears to outweigh any higher rate of transpiration which might be expected to occur in the dry evergreen forest. The next step in environmental degradation, the savanization of the biotope, has less impact on soil water reserves but, nevertheless, should be avoided regarding other ecological consequences. Progression of the deforested area around the Upper Shaba mining towns by charcoal and firewood production  today the woodland, for 70 km around Lubumbashi, is threatened with destruction, whilst an area of 30 km radius has already been completely cleared-out  has alarming consequences, notably decrease of biomass production, rise of the mean annual temperature and of the mean daily amplitude. 20793684|Une grande partie du calcium des feuilles ne peut plus intervenir de faon directe dans le mtabolisme du cytoplasme, parce qu'il a t inactiv par:  une prcipitation sous forme d'oxalate de calcium;  une complexation par des acides organiques (malique, citrique);  une fixation  l'extrieur du protoplasme (en partie sous forme d'uronates). Le rle physiologique du calcium, et la nature essentiellement passive de son absorption par les plantes sont discuts  la lumire de l'existence de ces mcanismes d'inactivation. La typologie d'Iljin et Kinzel a t amende sur quelques points:  les monocotyldones ont t spares des autres plantes suprieures, partant du fait que leurs pectates reprsentent habituellement moins de 50% des fonctions uroniques totales;  Iljin et Kinzel distinguent deux types de plantes selon qu'elles ont dans leur suc un excs en oxalates (calciophobes) ou en calcium (calciotrophes); chez Geranium robertianum, nous avons trouv aprs la soustraction du calcium fix dans les espaces extra-protoplasmiques un excs en oxalate qui n'est pas rvl par les mthodes d'analyse appliques par Iljin et Kinzel. The physiological role of calcium and the passive nature of its absorption has been discussed, according to the existence of these inactivation mechanisms. The physiological typology of Iljin and Kinzel has been reviewed. Two new types were added:  The monocotyledons have been separated from the other superior plants on the fact that their pectates usually represent less than 50% of the total uronic functions.  Iljin and Kinzel distinguish two types of plants, one containing an excess of soluble oxalate (calciophobes) the other having an excess of calcium (calciotrophes). In Geranium robertianum after substraction of the calcium fixated in the extraprotoplasmic process, we have found an excess of oxalate which was not revealed by the analytical methods used by Iljin and Kinzel. We propose to use the term "cryptocalciophobes" for this type of plant.

20792498|Gibberellic acid (GA) is applied on three species grown in non-inductive conditions for flowering: Rudbeckia bicolor (a long-day plant), Perilla nankinensis (a short-day plant) and Apium graveolens (a cold-requiring plant). The morphological and histological changes induced by GA have been investigated simultaneously. In the three species tested, stem elongation is enhanced. The histological results have shown that the stimulation of DNA synthesis and mitotic activity within the subapical pith is the prerequisite for the action of GA on stem growth. Moreover, the percentage of transverse divisions is always increased in the pith. The GA-induced flowering in Rudbeckia is linked to a selective stimulation of DNA synthesis and mitotic activity within the central zone of the apical meristem. In Perilla, GA reduces the plastochron length by stimulating DNA synthesis and mitotic activity within the peripheral zone of the meristem. Leaf area in Apium is greatly enhanced by GA application. This effect is not related to an action of the hormone upon the apical meristem of the shoot, but is probably linked to an action upon the apical and marginal meristems of the leaves. It is thus shown that a particular morphogenetic effect of GA may be ascribed to an action of this substance upon one particular zone or tissue within the shoot apex or within the leaf primordium. The specificity of histological reactions is reflected by the specificity of morphological responses.

20792822|The spoilheap n 7 left at Chapelle-lez-Herlaimont by the Mariemont-Bascoup coal-mine which closed down in 1955, has become one of the most verdant of the area (southern part of the belgian coal-bed - Charleroi). A rapid survey of this particular spoilheap's vegetation enabled us to point out not only an unexpected diversity of the flora (for instance: 7 species of Hieracium, 6 species of Epilobium, 6 species and subspecies of Poa, 4 species of ferns, 3 species of orchids, 2 species of Pyrola, 2 species of Aira, etc.), but also a great diversity of biotopes and plant communities. The most recent spoils, especially the more or less loose S and W slopes are now being colonized by xerophytic pioneer vegetation mainly composed of Teucrium scorodonia, Epilobium lanceolatum, Hieracium pilosella, Agrostis tenuis, etc. The plateau and the stabilized N and E slopes, on the other hand, are covered with coppice of birch (Betula pendula and B. pubescens) and sallow (Salix caprea). Several forest communities can be recognized with reference to the nature of the substratum (pure shales, shales + cindres or slag, pulverulent ashes), the topography and the time of the forestation. The first measurements of the forest productivity in two communities with nettle undergrowth (Urtica dioica) give from 8 to 9 t dry matter/ha/year, for the herbaceous layer and tree leaves only.

20792612|The tip of the pulp factory of Mont-Saint-Guibert is made up of the accumulation of CaCO produced at the end of the cycle of pulp fabrication when the caustic soda (NaOH) which serves to cook the wood is regenerated. The fresh mud has a pH higher than 12 because of the presence of slaked lime (Ca(OH)) and caustic soda (NaOH). The analyses show that with time a chemical evolution is produced with the mud which progressively carbonizes and bi-carbonizes downwards from the surface. The plant colonization of the spreading mud is related to this chemical evolution. It begins with the chlorophytes, followed by the mosses, and after three to four years by a species generally considered as halophilous, Puccinellia distans (L.) Parl. The dispersion and the ecology of this plant is discussed. The last stage of the colonization is marked by the arrival of a series of ubiquitous species and finishes by the forestation of the tip.

20792469|Four concentrations of a Lens roots extract and of a Salvia leaves extract have been comparatively studied as to their oxidative capacity on DOPA, in presence and without HO. The Lens' peroxidasic activity is more important than the phenoloxidasic activity. The inverse is true for Salvia. When IAA is incubated with Lens' extracts, it disappears progressively and it has been shown it gives degradation products. When it is incubated with Salvia, a part of the initial quantity only is revealed colorimetrically at zero time; it becomes revelable during the incubation: it has not been destroyed so. Moreover the Salvia extract inhibits IAA destruction by Lens. The substances in Salvia which mask auxin coloration and provoque the auxinoxidasic inhibition must be polyphenolic compounds. Indeed catechol or pyrogallol, for examples, prevent at once auxin coloration and auxin catabolism. IAA measured during a reaction of catechol oxidation by a tyrosinase first disappears promptly but reappears slowly in course of time. It is suggested that the IAA inactivations by phenol-oxidasic extracts previously reported must simply be explained by formation of auxin-phenol and auxin-quinone complexes. Realisation of such complexes does not seem involve enzyme. But, by oxidating phenols, the phenoloxidasic enzymes modify their effector power on IAA-oxidase and so indirectly participate to the auxin-oxidase activity.

20792824|Using a transect complex intentionally chosen in a hilly area on various bed-rocks (wooded bend of the Lomme river across devonian limestone and schist in the Eprave-Rochefort region  Southeast Belgium), an attempt is made to determine the main ecological groups (according to Duvigneaud, 1946, 1961, 1970) which compose the forest vegetation of the Calestienne region ( ecological sector of Calestienne  according to Galoux, 1962, 1967). Twelve ecological groups were distinguished and ecologically defined on the basis of the environmental conditions (climate and soil conditions, namely fertility and moisture) best expressed as humus types (Duchaufour, 1957) which provide the denominations of the corresponding ecological groups: calcic Mull group; poly-, mso-, oligotrophic Mull groups; Moder group; Mor group; etc. Among these, the calcic Mull group (including the  calcithermophyte  species) is particularly well developed and typical of the ecological sector, whereas the more or less acidophytic groups are considered to be  marginal  since they are essentially distributed on silicious ground. This ecological group system is not fundamentally different from those first elaborated for the Belgian Lorraine and the Semois valley (Tanghe, 1967 and 1968).

20794100|Differentiation between populations of the annual autogamous species Petrorhagia prolifera (Caryophyllaceae) has been investigated. Populations located at the western border of the distribution area (Belgium, Northern France) are compared with more central European populations used as controls. Little acid phosphatase variation within and between populations has been observed for acid phosphatase electrophoretic variants. Conversely, a great deal of morphological differentiation occurs in leaf size between populations but without clear relation to the ecological or geographical origin of the populations. However, in a few populations from Belgian coal mine tips, small epidermal tubercules are sometimes present on the ventral face of the seeds. The occurrence of this character, which does not occur in the other European populations studied, is discussed for its evolutionary significance. 20794014|Les basse tempratures (0-10C) provoquent un jaunissement des feuilles, elles rduisent la respiration et abaissent le taux de photosynthse. Ce dernier effet n'est pas li apparemment au syndrome C4 et des controverses existent dans la littrature quant au rle jou par diffrents enzymes dans cette diminution de la photosynthse. L'effet le plus rapide d'une diminution de la temprature du sol, sur les parties ariennes, consiste en l'arrt ou le ralentissement marqu de la croissance des feuilles et des pseudotiges, suite  l'action directe de la temprature sur les rgions mristmatiques. La diminution du potentiel hydrique des parties ariennes qui rsulte de l'action de la temprature sur le systme radiculaire pourrait aussi jouer un rle (rle mineur en champ). Les basses tempratures qui rgnent dans le sol au printemps ralentissent ou inhibent la croissance et le dveloppement du systme radiculaire. Elles diminuent l'absorption, par ce dernier, de l'eau et des lments minraux provoquant une carence minrale et une rduction du potentiel hydrique au niveau des parties ariennes. Elles ont galement pour consquence d'augmenter les risques d'apparition, chez les jeunes plantules, d'intoxication ammoniacale. Il existe de nombreuses relations entre les diffrents effets du froid sur les parties ariennes et les racines. La croissance du mas  basse temprature semble plus limite par une diminution de l'longation et de la division cellulaire que par la photosynthse. Une tude plus dtaille des mcanismes de base affectant ces processus devrait permettre de mieux cerner le problme de la croissance du mas  basse temprature. Low temperatures during juvenile growth result in a yellowing of leaves and a reduction of respiration and photosynthesis. The fastest effect of a reduction of soil temperature on the shoot is a complete stop or a drastic slowing down of the growth of laminae and pseudostems, due to a direct action of temperature on meristems. A decrease of water potential of the shoot, due to an effect of low temperatures on the roots could also play a role but this is minor in field conditions. Growth and development of the root system is also reduced. Water and mineral uptake by the root system is diminished resulting in mineral deficiencies and water stress in the shoot. Risks of ammonium intoxication increase. Effects of low temperatures on roots and shoots are interrelated. Growth of maize at low temperatures during the juvenile stage seems to be more limited by cell elongation and cell division than by photosynthesis. More detailed studies of the effect of low temperatures on cell elongation and division in maize are needed.

20793799|The equation S = CAz (S = number of species on an area A; C and z = positive constants), has been used to calculate the species-area relation of the Belgian flora. The data used for calculation are the mean number of species on 16 km and the total number of species of the Belgian flora. The relation for the Belgian flora is S = 151 A0,216. Values for C and z are different for the Atlantic and the Mid-european part of Belgium, but the z values fall between the 95% -confidence limits of the value for the European relationship based on regression (S = 168A0,222). This equation, the "standard-line" of the Dutch authors, needs great care when using it for the evaluation of species richness. Species richness is not the only criterion for the selection of nature reserves, we disagree with the suggestion that habitats with fewer species than the relation suggests may be excluded from consideration as nature reserves. 20792764|The ecological groups of the Querceto-Coryletum ground flora from Ferage (Mesnil-glise near Dinant-Belgium), are distributed in well distinct concentric areas. The spreading of the groups is connected with the different humus forms of Mull type. The study of the soils water content and the observation of the water-level shows that these areas have different water regime; the infiltrating water is submitted to a lateral flow in the pedological layers. This lateral drainage happens following a main south-north direction and so maintains a water supply in the lowest parts of the studied forest. The lateral drainage is due to the slope (about 3% north and west) and to the higher clay content of the B and B/C horizons of the soil. In the Ferage forest, water regime of the soil is an important ecological factor for the generation and the distribution of the humus types and their corresponding ecological groups of the ground flora.

20792753|Self-sustained oscillations of membrane potentials in Nitella cells.  When the ratio of different ions is varied in the external solution but the total concentration kept constant at 2 mM, the both membrane potentials of Nitella cells sometimes exhibit after a short delay some oscillations. The firing pattern consists of spontaneous and self-sustained periodical voltage changes or potential spikes of varying amplitude and duration. This phenomenon is uncommon but a pretreatment with D.C.M.U. (which inhibits system II of photosynthesis) increases its frequence. The pattern of firing and the requirements for the generation of oscillations discard the assumption of repetitive action potentials. The empirical ressemblance of this periodic behaviour in Nitella to spontaneous oscillations in biochemical open systems far from thermodynamic equilibrium is discussed.
20793563|L'interaction kintine-acide abscissique a t tudie et compare  l'interaction kintine-coumarine au niveau de la croissance et des modifications du spectre des isoperoxydases. L'acide abscissique inhibe plus fortement la croissance des tiges que celle des racines,  l'inverse de ce qui s'observe pour la coumarine. Quoique la kintine puisse inhiber la croissance dans certains cas, elle contrecarre gnralement l'effet de l'ABA. Les effets combins kintine-coumarine semblent indiquer une action antagoniste entre ces deux facteurs. L'analyse des activits peroxydasiques totales ne fournit pas d'explication  ces phnomnes d'interaction. L'acide abscissique inhibe presque toutes les isoperoxydases dont l'activit est accrue par la kintine. Ceci indique que l'interaction kintine-ABA est non-spcifique. L'IAA et la coumarine influencent les mmes isoenzymes; il semblerait donc que la coumarine modifie le contenu endogne en auxine qui serait le vrai antagoniste de la kintine dans ce systme. The interaction between kinetin and abscisic acid was compared with that between kinetin and coumarin at the level of growth and changes in isoperoxidases. The previously described stronger inhibitory activity of ABA against shoot growth compared to root growth and the reverse for coumarin was confirmed. Kinetin while inhibitory to growth by itself in certain cases, counteracted ABA effect generally. The combined effects of kinetin and coumarin appeared to indicate that coumarin opposed the action of kinetin. An analysis of total peroxidase activity did not provide an explanation for these interactions. ABA inhibited nearly all isoperoxidases whose activities were enhanced by kinetin. This indicated that the interaction between these two compounds was non-specific. Kinetin and coumarin counteracted each other effect, more specifically on two isoenzymes. And as IAA and coumarin influenced the same isoenzymes, it would appear that coumarin modified the endogenous content of auxin which would be the true antagonist of kinetin in this system.

20792641|Contribution to the study of the wood of Tarrietia cochinchinensis Pierre.  The present publication deals with the problem of the technology of wood. In order to give a rational application of the wood Tarrietia cochinchinensis, we studied and determined the different characteristics of the wood: the anatomy, the physics, the mechanics and the natural durability. We also gave a short botanical description of the tree. The physical and mechanical properties were obtained by the method called  International . This method expresses the results by a humidity rate of 12%. The compression specimen measures 2 cm  2 cm  6 cm and the specimen of flexion measures 2 cm  2 cm  34 cm. The calculation is made according to the formula: $\frac{3}{2}\ \frac{\text{PL}}{\text{bh}^{2}}$. In order to examine the resistance of the wood against rotting, we exposed 48 specimens of dimensions: 5 cm  2,5 cm  1,5 cm to attack by the four test mushrooms for three months. The relative atmospheric humidity was 75% and the temperature was 22 C. We used twelve specimens for each mushroom. This attack causes a loss of dry weight, permitting an estimation of the degree of wood resistivity. We further studied the fabrication of the paper pulps. We used the process of Sulfate because we are of the opinion that this process gives better results than the process of Sulfite (N.S.S.C.) especially concerning the tropical woods. Finally, we treated the different possibilities of application for which this wood may be satisfying, considering the particularities from an anatomical as well as from a technological point of view.

20793817|Des essais mens en vue d'prouver l'influence de la dure et de la temprature des traitements prgerminatifs ont compar les effets d'un prtraitement unique  ceux qu'occasionnent la succession de deux prtraitements raliss  des tempratures diffrentes. Il en ressort que la postmaturation des aknes de Cladium mariscus (L.) Pohl. est loin d'tre aussi exigeante qu'il tait apparu jusqu'ici. En effet, la dormance de ces semences n'est pas absolue et peut tre plus ou moins bien leve dans une trs large gamme de conditions thermiques. Cependant, la postmaturation de la majorit des aknes exige l'action successive d'une priode chaude et d'une priode froide. Enfin, tout en respectant cette dernire condition, les prtraitements les plus favorables sont ceux qui ralisent la somme de temprature la plus leve dans les dlais les plus courts (trois mois  15 suivis d'un mois  10). Ce rsultat remet en cause, du moins pour l'espce tudie, la notion classique de dormance psychrolabile.  Effects of length of time treatments and of temperature treatments applied before germination tests were compared; particular attention was conceded to the effects of two different temperature treatments given one after another. It is shown that achenes afterripening does not exhibit such severe requirements as previously assessed. As a matter of fact seed dormancy is far from being absolute for it can be more or less relieved within a broad temperature range. However, afterripening of most of the achenes requires two successive temperature treatments, i.e. a heat treatment period followed by a chilling period. Finally, provided this last condition is enforced, the most suitable treatments are those caracterized by the highest sum of temperatures given within the shortest required time: three months at 15C followed by one month at 10C. That result implies, at least for the present species, a reconsideration of the classical concept of chilling relieved dormancy.

20792495|The activity of three isomers: l-threitol, d-threitol and (meso)erythritol-1,4-bis (methane sulfonate) was tested at the chromosome level. Vicia faba and Nigella damascena seeds were treated at several concentrations and first mitotic cycles were analysed in the root tips. It was shown that the l-isomer was much more efficient than the two others to induce chromosome aberrations in Vicia and Nigella, maximal differences being observed after the first mitotic cycle. Even at higher doses (320 mg/100 ml-3h) d-threitol and erythritol isomers were less effective than lower concentrations of the l-isomer on Vicia faba seeds. No significant difference was found for the d-threitol and erythritol isomers. For these two compounds, dose-effect relationship could not be established because of their too low activity. Cytological similarities suggest that these three compounds act by the same fundamental mechanism. Several hypothesis are proposed to explain the differences observed in the effectiveness of the substances.

20794159|The history of the lectotypification of Cyperus with C. esculentus is documented. 20794149|The Hansa Bay seagrass beds are quite distinct from those previously described in the South West Pacific and especially on the southern coast of Papua New Guinea. The dominant seagrasses are Halodule pinifolia between - 1 and - 6 m, Halodule uninervis between - 4 and - 7 m and locally Syringodium isoetifolium. Halophila ovalis s.l., Halophila minor and Halophila decipiens make smaller contributions to the total biomass; the first two species are found in the same areas as Halodules while Halophila decipiens is found alone and at greater depths. The distribution of the major species has been schematically mapped and their above- and underground biomass measured at several representative locations. The underground biomass is about three times higher than the aboveground biomass, the ratios for the individual species being close to those previously reported. A turnover of 25 days for leaves, with a production of 113 g dry weight/m/year, has been estimated for Halodule uninervis by the Zieman technique. Wave action seems to be the major factor limiting the seagrasses to the northern part of the bay and probably controlling the species composition and their distribution in depth. Given the small size of the species present and their relatively low density, biomass by m is low (48.7 g dry weight/m in the north of the bay) but the area occupied is important (probably more than 1.10 m), hence a total biomass we estimate to 45.10 g dry weight and a production of 132.10 g dry weight of leaves by year, which makes of Hansa Bay an important feeding ground for turtles and dugongs. Les espces dominantes sont Halodule pinifolia entre - 1 m et 6 m, H. uninervis entre - 4 et - 7 m et localement Syringodium isoetifolium. Halophila ovalis s.l., H. minor et H. decipiens apportent de plus petites contributions  la biomasse totale; les deux premires espces se trouvent dans les mmes zones que les Halodules, tandis que H. decipiens s'observe seul et  de plus grandes profondeurs. La distribution des espces principales a t cartographie schmatiquement et leur biomasse au-dessus du substrat et dans celui-ci a t mesure en plusieurs points reprsentatifs. Un renouvellement des feuilles en 25 jours, avec une production de 113 g/matire sche/m/an, a t estim pour Halodule uninervis en utilisant la technique de Zieman. 20794051|The influence of the pH of the medium upon the difference between the apparent proton extrusion (APE) through roots (as measured by the amount of base necessary to keep constant the pH of the medium) and the corrected proton extrusion (CPE i.e. the apparent extrusion corrected for the carbonate and bicarbonate neutralisation) has been studied with 7-days-old barley seedlings. The results show that at pH-values above 6 to 6.5, the amount of CO fixed by the mineral solution interferes with the APE-measurement. However, when the fixed CO is estimated separately and substracted from the APE-value we find a 1:1 ration between proton extrusion and cation uptake, whatever the pH of the medium. This fact gives further support to the model of ion uptake which has been proposed previously. La quantit de base ncessaire au maintien du pH du milieu de culture est une mesure de l'extrusion apparente de protons (APE) par les racines de plantules d'orge. Aux pH suprieurs  6, la base est partiellement utilise  la neutralisation du CO, ce qui entrane une surestimation de l'APE. Lorsque le CO fix est estim sparment et que cette valeur est soustraite de l'APE, on obtient un rapport de 1:1 entre l'extrusion des protons et l'absorption des cations, quelque soit le pH du milieu. Ce fait confirme l'hypothse que nous avons propose pour expliquer l'absorption ionique.

20792683|Erica cinerea occurs South of Bruges (Belgium, Province of West-Flanders) in several communities of the Nardo-Callunetea. It is of little importance in the heaths with much Calluna vulgaris belonging to the Calluneto-Genistetum typicum (Txen, 1937). Its optimal habitats are found on somewhat disturbed places where it occurs in a grassy heath: the Calluneto-Sieglingietum (Heinemann, 1949) Ericetosum cinereae sub. ass. nov. The species is also very common in the grass vegetations of the Nardo-Galion, i. e. the Galio hercynici-Festucetum (Rasch, 1963) and the Pedicularetum sylvaticae (Van Andel et Waterbolk, 1946). On the other hand Erica cinerea has been found on several occasions under plantations of Pinus and Picea. In this habitat it is of greater importance than Calluna. Carex binervis, another atlantic species has been noted in some localities, although his most abondant stations are to be found out of the Erica cinerea area. The above mentioned vegetations are now mainly restricted to roadsides through the woods and parts of the arable land. Through land reclamation, restructuration and the increasing use of herbicides and fertilizers, Erica cinerea dissapeared out of at least 15 km where it was observed before.
20794068|De vestingsgrachten van Damme zijn de resten van een dubbele rij van grachten, in de 17de eeuw aangelegd in de vorm van een zevenster rond Damme. Een vegetatiestudie volgens de Braun-Blanquet-methode, aangevuld met systematisch gekozen opnamen, leverde 4 gemeenschappen op. Twee gemeenschappen nemen het grootste deel van het gebied in: een gemeenschap gedomineerd door Carex paniculata (moerasbos), die zich min of meer spontaan ontwikkelde en een gemeenschap van Phragmites australis die gedurende lange tijd beheerd geweest is. In het rietland heeft zich Salix  multinervis en Alnus glutinosa gevestigd en lokaal komt er een gemeenschap van Carex pseudocyperus en een gemeenschap van Typha angustifolia voor. Het verminderen van de oppervlakte van het rietland en het ontstaan en de uitbreiding van de Carex pseudocyperus-vegetatie worden hoofdzakelijk veroorzaakt door de activiteit van muskusratten (Ondatra zibethicus). De partile regressie (het afsterven van bomen door zomerdroogte en andere verstoringen) in de vegetatietypen gedomineerd door Carex paniculata wordt besproken. Tenslotte wordt ook op het natuurhistorisch belang van de vestingsgrachten van Damme en op het te voeren beheer gewezen. The moats of Damme are the remainder of a double belt of moats constructed in the form of a heptagon around Damme in the 17th century. Until the middle of the 19th century these ditches probably remained open water. Since then some parts have been filled up, but in most of the moats a natural succession took place. On the basis of 75 Braun-Blanquet-vegetation relevs 4 major vegetation types have been identified. Their relationships have been studied using the unweighted pair-group cluster method. Structural diversity has been illustrated by vegetation profiles and a vegetation map. Two communities occupy the major part of the area: a community dominated by Carex paniculata (swamp forest) and a community of Phragmites australis. The former developed more or less spontaneously and consists of a more or less floating mat of large Carex paniculata tussocks; its subdivision is based on fern and tree species. In contrast, the reedmarsh has been managed for a long time preventing a further succession. Locally the reedbeds have been invaded by Salix  multinervis and to some extent also by Alnus glutinosa; a community of Carex pseudocyperus and a community of Typha angustifolia also occur locally. Partial regression resulting in tree mortality in the vegetation type dominated by Carex paniculata as a consequence of summer drought and other disturbances is discussed. The decline of the reedmarsh and the origin and expansion of Carex pseudocyperus-vegetation mainly results from the effects of muskrats (Ondatra zibethicus). Finally the importance and the management of the moats of Damme for nature conservation are assessed.

Les valeurs absolues par contre sont  peine plus leves pour le manganse. Il est en effet difficile de retracer l'origine du Fe et du Mn dans les stations de Trapa, le minralisation par ces deux lments pouvant tre dues  la dcomposition de Trapa lui-mme. Trapa natans L. ssp. verbanensis (De Not.) Schinz has been collected from one of its six stations in southern Lake Maggiore, and analysed for Ca, Mg, Mn, Fe, Na, K and SiO. The results clearly show that this plant is able to accumulate manganese and iron in its pinnate roots (Mn:1,36% and Fe:3,51%). The least concentrations were measured in the albumen (Mn:12 ppm and Fe:87 ppm). The Fe/Mn ratio progressively decreases from 2,6 in the roots to 0,5 in the leaves where manganese is selectively accumulated. In the water and sediment from Trapa stations, the Fe/Mn ratio was found to be higher than in other stations in Lake Maggiore, whereas the absolute manganese concentrations are only scarcely higher than the mean of the lake. Although the analysis show Trapa is able to accumulate manganese, they do not confirm the Trapa-manganese geobotanical association reported in Russian literature. Moreover, the higher manganese and especially iron concentrations might well be due to the decomposing Trapa itself.

20792615|We have studied, by means of the optical microscope, the morphology of some samples of wood (Larix and Betula) destroyed by fungi and collected in the environs of Darmstadt (Germany).
