20793564|L'existence des phytoagglutinines ou lectines dans des graines ou des tubercules donne  rflchir  la raison de cette distribution dans les organes de rserve. Sauf exception, les tudes de ces protines au point de vue chimique, ont nglig d'envisager la physiologie de l'organe dont elles sont extraites. Il est sans doute fondamental de multiplier les tudes o la protine est caractrise en fonction du cycle de vie de la plante. Nous avons montr ici que l'activit rythroagglutinante d'extraits contenant la lectine de pomme de terre, est fonction de la zone de tissu de l'organe tubris et du degr d'incubation. Le manque d'effet agglutinant mis en vidence  la priphrie de l'organe de rserve correspond  un inhibiteur de l'action de la lectine. Les extraits de germes au stade polygerminal non ramifi, n'ont pas d'effet agglutinant. Celui-ci apparat plus tard, lorsque les germes ont atteint le stade polygerminal ramifi alors que l'activit agglutinante est restaure dans la zone de tissu priphrique. Cette dernire observation est valable aussi bien pour les tubercules germant normalement que pour ceux qui ont subi un traitement antigerminatif (phnylcarbamate). Il faut conclure que l'apparition de l'activit agglutinante est lie non au stade de germination mais bien au degr d'incubation des tubercules aprs la rcolte. De plus, plusieurs modalits d'extraction correspondant  diverses activits agglutinantes sont discutes. The existence of phytoagglutinins or lectins in seeds or in tubers raises the question about the distribution in these plants parts. With certain exceptions the chemical studies have neglected to consider the physiology of the organs from which these proteins are extracted. It is necessary to extend the studies in order to characterize these proteins as they function in the life of the plant. We have shown here, using potato extracts, that the erythroagglutinating activity is a function of tissue location in the tubers and of the time of incubation. The absence of an observable agglutinating effect in the peripheral tissue is caused by the presence of a lectin inhibitor. The extracts of sprouts, at the stage in which they are not ramified, have no agglutinating activity. This activity appears later when the sprouts have reached the ramified polygerminal stage; at this time also the agglutinating activity appears in the peripheral tissue. This observation applies to the normal potato as well as to those which have been treated with an antigerminant (phenylcarbamate). It must be concluded that agglutinating activity is associated with the incubation time and not with the sprouting stage. Also discussed here are several methods of extraction which lead to different observed agglutinating activities.

20794057|From the comparison of the vegetation developed on high termite mounds in Upper Shaba in dry evergreen forest, woodland and wooded savanna environment arises the fact that the first vegetation type possesses the largest number of peculiar woody plants. Basal area shows weak differences (31.1 to 24.3), highest figures occuring in woodland where three tree species are easily dominant: Haplocoelum foliolosum, Combretum collinum and Boscia corymbosa. The global synthesis at the three biotopes level confirms that basal area is a useful approach towards their distinction. Available ground water and above all fire are the main driving forces controlling the evolution of Upper-Shaban vegetation. La comparaison de la vgtation observe sur les hautes termitires au Shaba mridional en fort dense sche, en fort claire et en savane boise montre que le premier milieu prsente le nombre d'essences propres le plus lev. La surface terrire est dans l'ensemble peu variable (31,1  24,3), les valeurs les plus leves tant notes en fort claire o dominent nettement trois espces: Haplocoelum foliolosum, Combretum collinum et Boscia corymbosa. La synthse globale au niveau de ces trois milieux confirme que la surface terrire constitue une critre utile pour leur distinction. La savane boise de la Luiswishi se distingue des savanes boises ouest-africaines et sud-africaines par une plus grande diversit spcifique et surtout par le plus grand nombre d'espces ligneuses importantes. Les rserves en eau du sol et surtout le feu sont les facteurs fondamentaux orientant l'volution de la vgtation au Shaba mridional.

P. nodosus est une espce  vaste distribution, rpandue des les Aores et Canaries jusqu' l'gypte; il se trouve galement en Afrique occidentale, au Soudan,  Socotra, ainsi qu' Madagascar. P. thunbergii est une espce strictement africaine, prsente en thiopie, au Zare, au Rwanda, au Burundi, en Afrique orientale et australe, et peut-tre  Madagascar. Aucun pays, sauf peuf-tre Madagascar, ne possde  la fois P. nodosus et P. thunbergii dans sa flore. Obermeyer (1966) a,  juste titre, plac P. richardii dans la synonymie de P. thunbergii, mais certains caractres qu'elle signale comme distinguant P. thunbergii de P. nodosus ne sont pas constants. An examination of bibliographical data and of the identifications noted on Potamogeton herbarium material from Africa reveals a very confused knowledge of the distribution of P. nodosus and P. thunbergii. Anatomical study of numerous herbarium specimens allowed the authors to establish the distribution in Africa of these species. P. nodosus is a species with an extensive distribution, widespread from the Azores and Canary Islands to Egypt; it occurs also in West Africa, Sudan, Socotra, and Madagascar. P. thunbergii is a strictly African species, present in Ethiopia, Zare, Rwanda, Burundi, Eastern and Southern Africa, and perhaps in Madagascar. No country, except possibly Madagascar, has both P. nodosus and P. thunbergii in its flora. Obermeyer (1966) has rightly placed P. richardii as a synonym of P. thunbergii, but certain characteristics she mentions as distinguishing P. thunbergii from P. nodosus are not constant. These species differ from each other in their chromosome numbers: P. nodosus has 2n = 52 chromosomes; for P. thunbergii, we found 2n = 42 (the number also found by Stern in the closely related P. natans).

20792763|Investigations on dormancy in Rosa. Relation between the maturation of achenes on the mother-plant and their state of dormancy.  The hips of two Rose species, Rosa laxa Retz and Rosa canina 'Pfnder', were gathered every 15 days between the end of Augustus and the end of November. The fresh achenes are immediately stratified under two different conditions: directly at 2 C or first 4 1/2 months at 20 C before transfer into 2 C. By the first method, the required after-ripening time for maximal germination is the same for the achenes collected at various dates (5 and 6 months respectively for R. laxa and R. canina 'Pfnder') but the percentages of germination are quite different: the achenes of the first harvested ones do not germinate and the achenes from subsequent harvest show values of germination progressively higher with a maximum for the achenes gathered in the first days of October. After this date, the maturation of hips on mother-plant impose a deeper dormancy: the achenes of the two species germinate poorly compared to those harvested earlier. The high temperature pretreatment do not modify qualitatively this evolution of states of dormancy, but increase the maximum percentage of germination of the achenes of various harvest. This kind of after-ripening treatment enables to germinate the achenes harvested at the first date.
20793514|Barley seedlings where grown during six days on calcium salt solution differing in their accompanying anion. A way to estimate the concentration of mobile calcium in roots and to caculate the rate of absorption and transport of calcium to the shoots is given. The results show a wide variation of both calculated quantities with the different anions present. According to Pitman (1964), the hypothesis is made that the movement of the calcium cations through the root cortex is limited by the mobility of the accompanying anions which are hindered by the presence of immobile negative charges in the cortex. A correlation between the concentration of mobile negative calcium in the roots or the rate of absorption-transport of calcium to the shoots and the difference between the electrolytic ion mobilities of the calcium cation and his accompanying anion, is demonstrated. However this relation is not simple, it is possible to deduce, that the limiting effect of the accompanying anion on the absorption of calcium is greater, the more its electrolytic mobility in aqueous solutions is great.

20792765|Mineralization of organic matter is studied by incubating humus from different associations of the Ferage Oak-hazel forest (Mesnil-glise, near Dinant, Belgium); a ruderal zone with Urtica dioica and a adjoining grassland are also selected for comparison. The humus samples are incubated in laboratory at 25 C during eight weeks. Mull samples of the north slope, the plateau (Oak-hazel association with Ranunculus ficaria and/or Lamium galeobdolon), the ruderal part and the grassland show a low production of N.NH and a high production of N.NO; the contrary happens for the acid Mull (Oak-hazel association with Poa nemoralis) and Moder (Oak association with Deschampsia flexuosa) of the south slope. So, very important differences in organic nitrogen mineralization are found in the humus type of the same forest. The humus forms of the Ferage forest result from a differenciated water regime, as showed before (Froment, Schnock et Tanghe, 1970).

20792850|Periodical fluctuations of the moisture content of principal species composing the herbaceous layer and of the strata of mosses during the year 1969.  Investigations on the water content of twelve species from the herbaceous layer of a mixed oak forest have shown that it varies from 100 to 1100% during the year 1969. For Scilla bifolia and Narcissus pseudonarcissus, variation in water content extents from 550 to 1100%, for Lamium galeobdolon, Viola reichenbachiana, Fragaria vesca and Carex digitata from 150 to 700% and for Hedera helix, from 100 to 300%. Highest values are observed during the flowering time in S. bifolia, N. pseudonarcissus, Primula veris and L. galeobdolon, during the foliar infolding for Mercurialis perennis and Fagus sylvatica (cotyledonal leaves) and during the fruiting period for F. vesca, and V. reichenbachiana. For the species with vegetative reproduction (F. vesca, L. galeobdolon and C. digitata), the water content reaches high percentages during this whole period. The moistering percentage of the mosses layer (internal plus external water) depends more on the rainfalls distribution than on the phenology of the species: 60% in dry period and 470% after rainy weather. The mean water content (mm) of the ground flora is lower than 1 mm and shows considerable variations which reache 50% (0,4 mm) of the mean value. These variations are due to extreme values observed in the mosses which are able to store 0,16 mm of rainfalls and to evapotranspire 90% of it after a few dry days. More than 80% of this water are kept within H. helix when L. galeobdolon, M. perennis and V. reichenbachiana at their optimal growth only content 10 to 15% (0,1 mm), A. nemorosa: 0,03 mm and S. bifolia: 0,01 mm.

20792497|Hordeum sativum, Vicia faba and Nigella damascena dry seeds were treated successively by HgCl and EMS. Mercuric chloride increased significantly the effects of ethyl methane sulfonate on chromosomes. The effects of EMS alone are usually low. Post-treatments with 2,3-dimercaptopropanol (BAL) suppressed the synergism of the two chemicals. The results indicate that mercuric ions act by inhibiting enzymatic systems bearing -SH radicals. The inhibition of these substances, as coenzyme A, ATPase or some deshydrogenases could modify the bioenergetics of the cell leading to chromosome aberrations.

20794180|The mangrove of Gazi Bay (at approximately 50 km south of Mombasa) is not directly under the influence of freshwater: the two small rivers discharging in the bay are seasonal and seepage is restricted to some points. 20792844|Hydrogen peroxide effects on Douglas-fir germinative processes.  The germination of Douglas-fir seeds in a 1% hydrogen peroxide solution occurs at a fast and hight rate. This treatment is the most effective when HO solution quickly and intimately comes in contact with the endosperm and the embryo. Even more, HO has to operate the whole germinative processes long and does not drastically overcome the inhibitory effects imposed by seed coats. It is not through a release of oxygen that HO promotes germination for an increase of the pure O external pressure does not in any way improve the results. Consequently, the beneficial effects of HO arise from a direct stimulation of the endosperm-and/or embryo-metabolism.

20794011|Morphology and cytotype of wood and grassland populations of Cardamine pratensis L. s.l. from Belgium and northern France have been studied. The wood populations are diploid (2n = 16) and correspond with Cardamine pratensis L. subsp. picra De Langhe & D'hose. 20793461|During five days of summer and fall 1970, total solar radiation (300-3000 nm) and visible light (300-780 nm) were measured by means of pyranometers and photometers at the same time in a 140-year-old beech-grove (Fagus sylvatica L.), in a 56-year-old spruce plantation (Picea abies (L.) Karst.) and in the open, at the "Plateau des Tailles" in Belgian "Haute-Ardenne". On clear days, the deciduous canopy reduces incoming solar radiation in an average proportion of 91%; for the conifers, the value is 95%; the leafless deciduous canopy shuts off only 71%. Visible light is more restricted than the total solar radiation: its reduction reaches 97.5% in the beech-stand and 99% in the conifer stand. The reduction of solar radiation seems to be greater on clear weather than on cloudy or overcast conditions. The study of the relationship between solar radiation and visible light shows that the proportion of "long-wave" radiation (780-3000 nm) is greater in the forest stands, specially in the beech-grove, than in the open.

From the heathland soils emerged Juncus effusus, Juncus bulbosus, Erica tetralix and Calluna vulgaris. Agrostis canina and Luzula multiflora were more prominent in soils from the mown or grazed heath. The species noted in the heathland soils survived in soils of 20 yr. old improved grassland. They were absent in the grasslands reclaimed before 1940. The above ground vegetation and the buried seeds show a strong correlation but only a reduced similarity. The development of the vegetation depends merely on the available flora of the site, part of which is sometimes present as viable seeds only. Agrostis canina et Luzula multiflora taient plus abondantes sous les landes herbeuses. 20793471|The absorption and the localisation of calcium was studied by barley seedlings (Hordeum distichum L. cultivar Mosane) cultivated on demineralised water or calcium sulfate 0,25.10 M. The calcium sulfate solution was applied during 0, 1, 2, 3 or 5 days at the beginning or at the end of the experimental period. An analysis of the growth responses and the calcium concentrations leads to the conclusion that:  calcium has an inhibitory effect on the development of the root-apex meristem but influences favorably the growth of the differenciation and the elongation zones.  the total absorption of calcium requires: a) an absorption directly correlated with root growth and irreversibly fixed in cellular structures b) a passive permeation of calcium through the root cortex to the endodermis c) an active transport accross the endodermis to the stele followed by a translocation to the aerial parts of the plant.
20792678|Nous avons tudi certains aspects de la morphologie et du dveloppement des verticilles d'Acetabularia mediterranea. Ils sont constitus par des poils polychotomiques qui possdent une surface 2-4 fois plus grande que celle du siphon tout entier. Ce fait semble suggrer que les verticilles pourraient tre impliqus dans l'absorption de la lumire et peut-tre de certaines substances nutritives dissoutes dans l'eau de mer. Les poils des verticilles montrent parfois des modifications importantes dans leur morphologie. Ils peuvent galement contenir des cystes mrs tout  fait identiques  ceux du chapeau. Des expriences de marquage avec des prcurseurs du DNA, du RNA et des protines ont montr que le cytoplasme (anucl) des verticilles isols possde une importante activit mtabolique. We have studied some aspects of the morphology and development of the whorls in Acetabularia mediterranea. The whorls, which are constituted by very long polychotomic hairs, have a surface 2-4 times larger than that of the entire stalk. This fact seems suggest that they could play a role in light absorption and perhaps in the uptake of nutritive substances dissolved in sea-water. The hairs of the whorls sometimes show important modifications in their morphology. They can contain mature cysts identical to those of the cap. Labelling experiments with some precursors of DNA, RNA and proteins have shown that the (anucleated) cytoplasm of isolated whorls is metabolically very active.

20793570|A complex of wet and marshy meadows which have settled since at least 150 years on the eutrophic alluvial deposits of the Woluwe river, near the Hof-ter-Musschen in Woluw-Saint-Lambert (Brussels, Belgium), is studied from floristic and plant sociological angle. On a limited area of about 2 ha, the complex assembles a great number (about 150) of Phanerogam species of which several have become quite rare in the Brabantine valleys, and one, Triglochin palustris, extremely rare in Belgium. It also shows quite a number of different plant communities and soil types which at present have poor possibility of replacement, not only in the greater Brussels area, but also in the whole Picardo-Brabantine district. The best individualized plant communities are related to the Glycerio-Sparganion (Apium nodiflorum-Mentha aquatica community, Glyceria maxima community), the Magnocaricion elatae (Carex acutiformis community) and the Agropyro-Rumicion (Festuca rubra-Carex disticha-Triglochin palustris community).
20792292|Reviewing, by phytogeographical districts, the different localities where Liparis Loeselii has been encountered, the author cites for each of them the litterature and the herbarium specimens. It appears clearly from this that the species is in full decrease in Belgium. Known formerly from eighteen localities, distributed into three phytogeographical districts, it survives actually only at La Panne, Oostduinkerke and Anvers left bank all located in the maritime district, and at Neerpelt in the heath district. The main reasons for its gradual disappearance are: destroying of the marshes and bogs, extension of the sea-shore cities and extensive drainage. From a phytocenological viewpoint, the author considers L. Loeselii in Belgium as a characteristic of the Caricetalia fuscae, but not as an exclusive of the Caricion Davallianae.

20793723|L'excrtion de protons par le systme radiculaire de plantules d'orge a t mesure dans diffrentes conditions exprimentales et compare  l'absorption ionique concomittante. Les diffrences constates entre traitements peuvent s'expliquer par la plus ou moins grande richesse des racines en sucres solubles. Au cours de leur catabolisme, ces sucres engendrent non seulement l'acide carbonique gnrateur de protons, mais aussi l'ATP ncessaire  l'excrtion de ces derniers. Ces diffrences dans le pouvoir d'excrtion de protons ont  leur tour des rpercussions sur l'absorption ionique et, plus directement, sur l'absorption des cations monovalents. Extrusion of protons by barley roots has been measured in different experimental conditions. Differences in proton efflux may be attributed to the variable content of the roots in soluble sugars. During their catabolic breakdown, they not only produce carbonic acid, which generates protons, but also the ATP necessary for the proton extrusion. The differences in the capacity of excreting protons are paralleled by differences in ion uptake and more specifically in absorption of monovalent cations.

Scirpus cespitosus L. subsp. germanicus (Palla) Brod. has been known for a long time in Belgium. However it was only recently that the subsp. cespitosus was reported in the Hautes Fagnes area. This subspecies has just been found in the Plateau des Tailles. Field observations as well as laboratory studies allow a more complete and more accurate description of the differences between the two subspecies. An unequivocal identification in the field requires only an examination of the uppermost leaf and a comparison between the lamina length and the length of the sheath opening. A phytosociological table shows the presence of both subspecies in the bogs of the Plateau des Tailles and allows a determination of their specific ecological requirements.

20793943|La germination in vitro du pollen permet de juger ses aptitudes intrinsques  germer en dehors de toute interaction pollen-stigmate. De plus, ce test de viabilit est le meilleur et le plus fiable. Son utilisation localise rapidement une strilit mle partielle ou totale parmi une collection importante. Les essais permettent de constater le polymorphisme des grains de pollen qui germent; cette constatation est intressante pour les perspectives qu'elle laisse entrevoir pour l'amlioration des Fuchsia. In vitro pollen germination is the best test for pollen viability. Potentialities are verified without pollen-stigma interaction. Male sterility is rapidly detected in a collection. This study shows that amongst the irregular pollen grains, the germination is not linked to the pore number. This observation is important for further improvement of Fuchsia.
20792795|Effects of the sodium and potassium external concentration on the chloride electrochemical potential difference of Nitella.  The chloride electrochemical potential difference, membrane potential and electrical resistance of Nitella flexilis were measured at 3C and 20C in solutions where glucuronate is progressively substituted for chloride. The predominant cation is K or Na following the experiments but the ionic strength of the medium is kept constant at 1,1 mM. Cells pretreated in Ca-free medium are used throughout the experiments. The vacuolar concentrations are 64 mM K, 43 mM Na (flame photometry) and 80 mM Cl (electrotitrimetric titration). Membrane potential and resistance are little affected by variations of chloride in the external medium but large changes occur in the chloride electrochemical potential difference. The internal chloride concentration for the whole cell calculated from the values of these parameters decreases or increases with [Cl]o in an unexpected way with the reputed low permeability of the membrane to Cl ions. A double reciprocal plot of [Cl]i and [Cl]o for both the temperatures shows that the penetration of chlorides into Nitella is easier when Na is more abundant in the external medium and that this phenomenon is linked with the metabolic energy. The discrepancy between the chloride concentration measured by titration and microelectrode and the large variations of cellular chloride activity are discussed. The more likely explanation is that the thermodynamic active chlorides are only a part of the total chloride pool. The lack of effects on membrane potential is compared with the same stability observed when vacuolar sap is exchanged with artificial solutions where chlorides ions are varied.
20792655|Radiative and thermal fluxes of the forest were studied for a clear day. Radiative balance (Q) was determined by radiation measurements with Moll-Gorczynski thermopiles and Schulze radiometers. Soil heat flux (QG), vegetation heat flux (QV) and inner air layer heat flux (QL) were measured to obtain Qi (= QG + QV + QL) which is the heat flux in the active layers of the forest. Latent heat flux (V or evapotranspiration) and sensible heat flux (K or turbulent convection) were computed according to the Bowen's ratio and the heat budget method. Daily variations of each flux are presented in fig. 1 and 2. For a whole summer clear day, Q is 308,543 cal cm min and in percents of Q, evapotranspiration is 66,6%, turbulent convection 26,5%, whereas other fluxes are smaller: heat flux in the soil is 5,1%; in the vegetation 1,2%; and in the inner air layer only 0,6%.
20792631|Throughout the year and at five different levels on the current year shoots of apple and pear trees, buds were taken and isolated with a 7 cm-piece of stem and placed in moist sand. The capability of outgrowth of the buds was investigated. Different gradient-types were observed according with the time of the year. The behaviour of the buds was mainly affected by: 1) a summer inhibition related to the age of the bud, 2) a relative winter dormancy broken by chilling. In each case, the natural evolution thus described may lead to a kind of apical  precedence .
20792728|La microflore bactrienne (germes protolytiques, amylolytiques, cellulolytiques, fixateurs de N) et fongique est analyse pendant les annes 1967-1968 dans diffrents types de litire d'une chnaie  charme et d'une chnaie  coudrier. Bien qu'tant acides (pH: 4,3-5), les, litires de feuilles hbergent une importante flore bactrienne. Celle-ci est plus dense sur les feuilles de coudrier et de charme que sur les feuilles de chne ce qui correspond  une dcomposition plus rapide des deux premires litires. Les populations bactriennes des litires atteignent leur dveloppement maximum au cours des premiers mois de l'anne. L'abondance des fixateurs d'azote permet de supposer qu'ils pourraient intervenir effectivement dans les processus d'augmentation de la concentration d'azote observe par d'autres chercheurs au niveau de la litire. The bacterial and fungal microflora has been studied during 1967-1968 in litters in the oak forest on, mull (Querceto-Coryletum) near Ferage (Upper Belgium). Among the bacterial flora, proteolytic, amylolytic, celluloytic and nitrogen-fixing germs were considered. In spite of their acidity (pH: 4,3-5), the Corylus and Carpinus leaf litters are colonized by a large bacterial population. This one is more crowded on the Corylus and Carpinus leaf litters than on the oak leaf litters. That correlates with the faster decay of the two first ones. The bacterial populations of litters grow up to the maximum during the first months of the year. The abundance of Nitrogen-fixing germs should lead to the assumption that they could be effective in the N increase observed by others workers in litters, more especially as they could live in symbiosis with the numerous cellulolytic germs colonizing the dead leaves. Aureobasidium pullulans is the characteristic fungal pioneer of the Carpinus and Quercus litters. The yeasts concentration raises up to the maximum of 40.10 germs / dry gr. in the Quercus litter as well as in the Carpinus litter.

20794149|The Hansa Bay seagrass beds are quite distinct from those previously described in the South West Pacific and especially on the southern coast of Papua New Guinea. The dominant seagrasses are Halodule pinifolia between - 1 and - 6 m, Halodule uninervis between - 4 and - 7 m and locally Syringodium isoetifolium. Halophila ovalis s.l., Halophila minor and Halophila decipiens make smaller contributions to the total biomass; the first two species are found in the same areas as Halodules while Halophila decipiens is found alone and at greater depths. The distribution of the major species has been schematically mapped and their above- and underground biomass measured at several representative locations. The underground biomass is about three times higher than the aboveground biomass, the ratios for the individual species being close to those previously reported. A turnover of 25 days for leaves, with a production of 113 g dry weight/m/year, has been estimated for Halodule uninervis by the Zieman technique. Wave action seems to be the major factor limiting the seagrasses to the northern part of the bay and probably controlling the species composition and their distribution in depth. Given the small size of the species present and their relatively low density, biomass by m is low (48.7 g dry weight/m in the north of the bay) but the area occupied is important (probably more than 1.10 m), hence a total biomass we estimate to 45.10 g dry weight and a production of 132.10 g dry weight of leaves by year, which makes of Hansa Bay an important feeding ground for turtles and dugongs. 20794051|The influence of the pH of the medium upon the difference between the apparent proton extrusion (APE) through roots (as measured by the amount of base necessary to keep constant the pH of the medium) and the corrected proton extrusion (CPE i.e. the apparent extrusion corrected for the carbonate and bicarbonate neutralisation) has been studied with 7-days-old barley seedlings. The results show that at pH-values above 6 to 6.5, the amount of CO fixed by the mineral solution interferes with the APE-measurement. However, when the fixed CO is estimated separately and substracted from the APE-value we find a 1:1 ration between proton extrusion and cation uptake, whatever the pH of the medium. This fact gives further support to the model of ion uptake which has been proposed previously. La quantit de base ncessaire au maintien du pH du milieu de culture est une mesure de l'extrusion apparente de protons (APE) par les racines de plantules d'orge. Aux pH suprieurs  6, la base est partiellement utilise  la neutralisation du CO, ce qui entrane une surestimation de l'APE. Lorsque le CO fix est estim sparment et que cette valeur est soustraite de l'APE, on obtient un rapport de 1:1 entre l'extrusion des protons et l'absorption des cations, quelque soit le pH du milieu. Ce fait confirme l'hypothse que nous avons propose pour expliquer l'absorption ionique.

The evaluation of the reduction of chlorophyll content and growth points out the relative toxicity of Zn and Cd: growth of Chlorella was significantly delayed by 2.5 ppm Zn and by 0.75 ppm Cd. Based upon the criterion of chlorophyll content, the lethal doses 50 reach 13 ppm Zn and 2.1 ppm Cd. The effect of Zn was essentially marked on chlorophyll; it did not extend over one day and was not increased by concentrations superior to 20 ppm.

20792683|Erica cinerea occurs South of Bruges (Belgium, Province of West-Flanders) in several communities of the Nardo-Callunetea. It is of little importance in the heaths with much Calluna vulgaris belonging to the Calluneto-Genistetum typicum (Txen, 1937). Its optimal habitats are found on somewhat disturbed places where it occurs in a grassy heath: the Calluneto-Sieglingietum (Heinemann, 1949) Ericetosum cinereae sub. ass. nov. The species is also very common in the grass vegetations of the Nardo-Galion, i. e. the Galio hercynici-Festucetum (Rasch, 1963) and the Pedicularetum sylvaticae (Van Andel et Waterbolk, 1946). On the other hand Erica cinerea has been found on several occasions under plantations of Pinus and Picea. In this habitat it is of greater importance than Calluna. Carex binervis, another atlantic species has been noted in some localities, although his most abondant stations are to be found out of the Erica cinerea area. The above mentioned vegetations are now mainly restricted to roadsides through the woods and parts of the arable land. Through land reclamation, restructuration and the increasing use of herbicides and fertilizers, Erica cinerea dissapeared out of at least 15 km where it was observed before.
20794068|De vestingsgrachten van Damme zijn de resten van een dubbele rij van grachten, in de 17de eeuw aangelegd in de vorm van een zevenster rond Damme. Een vegetatiestudie volgens de Braun-Blanquet-methode, aangevuld met systematisch gekozen opnamen, leverde 4 gemeenschappen op. Twee gemeenschappen nemen het grootste deel van het gebied in: een gemeenschap gedomineerd door Carex paniculata (moerasbos), die zich min of meer spontaan ontwikkelde en een gemeenschap van Phragmites australis die gedurende lange tijd beheerd geweest is. In het rietland heeft zich Salix  multinervis en Alnus glutinosa gevestigd en lokaal komt er een gemeenschap van Carex pseudocyperus en een gemeenschap van Typha angustifolia voor. Het verminderen van de oppervlakte van het rietland en het ontstaan en de uitbreiding van de Carex pseudocyperus-vegetatie worden hoofdzakelijk veroorzaakt door de activiteit van muskusratten (Ondatra zibethicus). De partile regressie (het afsterven van bomen door zomerdroogte en andere verstoringen) in de vegetatietypen gedomineerd door Carex paniculata wordt besproken. Tenslotte wordt ook op het natuurhistorisch belang van de vestingsgrachten van Damme en op het te voeren beheer gewezen. The moats of Damme are the remainder of a double belt of moats constructed in the form of a heptagon around Damme in the 17th century. Until the middle of the 19th century these ditches probably remained open water. Since then some parts have been filled up, but in most of the moats a natural succession took place. On the basis of 75 Braun-Blanquet-vegetation relevs 4 major vegetation types have been identified. Their relationships have been studied using the unweighted pair-group cluster method. Structural diversity has been illustrated by vegetation profiles and a vegetation map. Two communities occupy the major part of the area: a community dominated by Carex paniculata (swamp forest) and a community of Phragmites australis. The former developed more or less spontaneously and consists of a more or less floating mat of large Carex paniculata tussocks; its subdivision is based on fern and tree species. In contrast, the reedmarsh has been managed for a long time preventing a further succession. Locally the reedbeds have been invaded by Salix  multinervis and to some extent also by Alnus glutinosa; a community of Carex pseudocyperus and a community of Typha angustifolia also occur locally. Partial regression resulting in tree mortality in the vegetation type dominated by Carex paniculata as a consequence of summer drought and other disturbances is discussed. The decline of the reedmarsh and the origin and expansion of Carex pseudocyperus-vegetation mainly results from the effects of muskrats (Ondatra zibethicus). Finally the importance and the management of the moats of Damme for nature conservation are assessed.

Moreover, the higher manganese and especially iron concentrations might well be due to the decomposing Trapa itself.

20793564|L'existence des phytoagglutinines ou lectines dans des graines ou des tubercules donne  rflchir  la raison de cette distribution dans les organes de rserve. Sauf exception, les tudes de ces protines au point de vue chimique, ont nglig d'envisager la physiologie de l'organe dont elles sont extraites. Il est sans doute fondamental de multiplier les tudes o la protine est caractrise en fonction du cycle de vie de la plante. Nous avons montr ici que l'activit rythroagglutinante d'extraits contenant la lectine de pomme de terre, est fonction de la zone de tissu de l'organe tubris et du degr d'incubation. Le manque d'effet agglutinant mis en vidence  la priphrie de l'organe de rserve correspond  un inhibiteur de l'action de la lectine. Les extraits de germes au stade polygerminal non ramifi, n'ont pas d'effet agglutinant. Celui-ci apparat plus tard, lorsque les germes ont atteint le stade polygerminal ramifi alors que l'activit agglutinante est restaure dans la zone de tissu priphrique. The existence of phytoagglutinins or lectins in seeds or in tubers raises the question about the distribution in these plants parts. With certain exceptions the chemical studies have neglected to consider the physiology of the organs from which these proteins are extracted. It is necessary to extend the studies in order to characterize these proteins as they function in the life of the plant. We have shown here, using potato extracts, that the erythroagglutinating activity is a function of tissue location in the tubers and of the time of incubation. The absence of an observable agglutinating effect in the peripheral tissue is caused by the presence of a lectin inhibitor. The extracts of sprouts, at the stage in which they are not ramified, have no agglutinating activity. This activity appears later when the sprouts have reached the ramified polygerminal stage; at this time also the agglutinating activity appears in the peripheral tissue. This observation applies to the normal potato as well as to those which have been treated with an antigerminant (phenylcarbamate). It must be concluded that agglutinating activity is associated with the incubation time and not with the sprouting stage. Also discussed here are several methods of extraction which lead to different observed agglutinating activities.

20793772|Le dpouillement des donnes bibliographiques et des identifications consignes dans les herbiers d'origine africaine du genre Potamogeton fait apparatre une connaissance trs confuse de la distribution de P. nodosus et de P. thunbergii. L'tude anatomique de nombreux spcimens d'herbier a permis aux auteurs de prciser la distribution africaine de ces espces. P. nodosus est une espce  vaste distribution, rpandue des les Aores et Canaries jusqu' l'gypte; il se trouve galement en Afrique occidentale, au Soudan,  Socotra, ainsi qu' Madagascar. P. thunbergii est une espce strictement africaine, prsente en thiopie, au Zare, au Rwanda, au Burundi, en Afrique orientale et australe, et peut-tre  Madagascar. Aucun pays, sauf peuf-tre Madagascar, ne possde  la fois P. nodosus et P. thunbergii dans sa flore. Obermeyer (1966) a,  juste titre, plac P. richardii dans la synonymie de P. thunbergii, mais certains caractres qu'elle signale comme distinguant P. thunbergii de P. nodosus ne sont pas constants. Les deux espces se distinguent par leur nombre chromosomique: P. nodosus a 2n = 52 chromosomes; pour P. thunbergii, nous avons trouv 2n = 42 (nombre galement trouv par Stern chez P. natans dont il est trs voisin). An examination of bibliographical data and of the identifications noted on Potamogeton herbarium material from Africa reveals a very confused knowledge of the distribution of P. nodosus and P. thunbergii. Anatomical study of numerous herbarium specimens allowed the authors to establish the distribution in Africa of these species. P. nodosus is a species with an extensive distribution, widespread from the Azores and Canary Islands to Egypt; it occurs also in West Africa, Sudan, Socotra, and Madagascar. P. thunbergii is a strictly African species, present in Ethiopia, Zare, Rwanda, Burundi, Eastern and Southern Africa, and perhaps in Madagascar. No country, except possibly Madagascar, has both P. nodosus and P. thunbergii in its flora. Obermeyer (1966) has rightly placed P. richardii as a synonym of P. thunbergii, but certain characteristics she mentions as distinguishing P. thunbergii from P. nodosus are not constant. These species differ from each other in their chromosome numbers: P. nodosus has 2n = 52 chromosomes; for P. thunbergii, we found 2n = 42 (the number also found by Stern in the closely related P. natans).

20792763|Investigations on dormancy in Rosa. Relation between the maturation of achenes on the mother-plant and their state of dormancy.  The hips of two Rose species, Rosa laxa Retz and Rosa canina 'Pfnder', were gathered every 15 days between the end of Augustus and the end of November. The fresh achenes are immediately stratified under two different conditions: directly at 2 C or first 4 1/2 months at 20 C before transfer into 2 C. By the first method, the required after-ripening time for maximal germination is the same for the achenes collected at various dates (5 and 6 months respectively for R. laxa and R. canina 'Pfnder') but the percentages of germination are quite different: the achenes of the first harvested ones do not germinate and the achenes from subsequent harvest show values of germination progressively higher with a maximum for the achenes gathered in the first days of October. After this date, the maturation of hips on mother-plant impose a deeper dormancy: the achenes of the two species germinate poorly compared to those harvested earlier. The high temperature pretreatment do not modify qualitatively this evolution of states of dormancy, but increase the maximum percentage of germination of the achenes of various harvest. This kind of after-ripening treatment enables to germinate the achenes harvested at the first date.
20793514|Barley seedlings where grown during six days on calcium salt solution differing in their accompanying anion. A way to estimate the concentration of mobile calcium in roots and to caculate the rate of absorption and transport of calcium to the shoots is given. The results show a wide variation of both calculated quantities with the different anions present. According to Pitman (1964), the hypothesis is made that the movement of the calcium cations through the root cortex is limited by the mobility of the accompanying anions which are hindered by the presence of immobile negative charges in the cortex. A correlation between the concentration of mobile negative calcium in the roots or the rate of absorption-transport of calcium to the shoots and the difference between the electrolytic ion mobilities of the calcium cation and his accompanying anion, is demonstrated. However this relation is not simple, it is possible to deduce, that the limiting effect of the accompanying anion on the absorption of calcium is greater, the more its electrolytic mobility in aqueous solutions is great.

20792765|Mineralization of organic matter is studied by incubating humus from different associations of the Ferage Oak-hazel forest (Mesnil-glise, near Dinant, Belgium); a ruderal zone with Urtica dioica and a adjoining grassland are also selected for comparison. The humus samples are incubated in laboratory at 25 C during eight weeks. Mull samples of the north slope, the plateau (Oak-hazel association with Ranunculus ficaria and/or Lamium galeobdolon), the ruderal part and the grassland show a low production of N.NH and a high production of N.NO; the contrary happens for the acid Mull (Oak-hazel association with Poa nemoralis) and Moder (Oak association with Deschampsia flexuosa) of the south slope. So, very important differences in organic nitrogen mineralization are found in the humus type of the same forest. The humus forms of the Ferage forest result from a differenciated water regime, as showed before (Froment, Schnock et Tanghe, 1970).

20792850|Periodical fluctuations of the moisture content of principal species composing the herbaceous layer and of the strata of mosses during the year 1969.  Investigations on the water content of twelve species from the herbaceous layer of a mixed oak forest have shown that it varies from 100 to 1100% during the year 1969. For Scilla bifolia and Narcissus pseudonarcissus, variation in water content extents from 550 to 1100%, for Lamium galeobdolon, Viola reichenbachiana, Fragaria vesca and Carex digitata from 150 to 700% and for Hedera helix, from 100 to 300%. Highest values are observed during the flowering time in S. bifolia, N. pseudonarcissus, Primula veris and L. galeobdolon, during the foliar infolding for Mercurialis perennis and Fagus sylvatica (cotyledonal leaves) and during the fruiting period for F. vesca, and V. reichenbachiana. For the species with vegetative reproduction (F. vesca, L. galeobdolon and C. digitata), the water content reaches high percentages during this whole period. The moistering percentage of the mosses layer (internal plus external water) depends more on the rainfalls distribution than on the phenology of the species: 60% in dry period and 470% after rainy weather. The mean water content (mm) of the ground flora is lower than 1 mm and shows considerable variations which reache 50% (0,4 mm) of the mean value. These variations are due to extreme values observed in the mosses which are able to store 0,16 mm of rainfalls and to evapotranspire 90% of it after a few dry days. More than 80% of this water are kept within H. helix when L. galeobdolon, M. perennis and V. reichenbachiana at their optimal growth only content 10 to 15% (0,1 mm), A. nemorosa: 0,03 mm and S. bifolia: 0,01 mm.

20793801|Phytosociological relevs and soil analyses for acidity and calcium carbonate content lead to a division of 6 common moss species and 9 common fern species into ecological groups, according to their soil preference. Calcicole, calcifuge, acidiphile, basiphile and indifferent species were distinguished. From further soil analyses (exchangeable Ca, Mg, K, Fe, Mn, Al, H) it has been concluded that especially Fe, Mn, Al and H could be responsible for the restriction of species to a certain substrate. Plant analyses (Ca, Mg, K, Na, Fe, Mn) showed that the cation content of the plants, though often dependent on the species, could not be related to the soil preference, except for the calcicole, basiphile species, that could be characterized by their low Mn-content. Les analyses d'autres facteurs du sol (Ca, Mg, K, Fe, Mn, Al, H changeables) ont montr que surtout Fe, Mn, Al et H pourraient jouer un rle dans la limitation d'une espce  un certain type de substrat. Verdere bodemanalyses (uitwisselbaar Ca, Mg, K, Fe, Mn, Al, H) toonden dat vooral Fe, Mn, Al en H in aanmerking komen als factoren die de soorten tot een bepaald substraat beperken. 20792497|Hordeum sativum, Vicia faba and Nigella damascena dry seeds were treated successively by HgCl and EMS. Mercuric chloride increased significantly the effects of ethyl methane sulfonate on chromosomes. The effects of EMS alone are usually low. Post-treatments with 2,3-dimercaptopropanol (BAL) suppressed the synergism of the two chemicals. The results indicate that mercuric ions act by inhibiting enzymatic systems bearing -SH radicals. The inhibition of these substances, as coenzyme A, ATPase or some deshydrogenases could modify the bioenergetics of the cell leading to chromosome aberrations.

20794180|The mangrove of Gazi Bay (at approximately 50 km south of Mombasa) is not directly under the influence of freshwater: the two small rivers discharging in the bay are seasonal and seepage is restricted to some points. 20792844|Hydrogen peroxide effects on Douglas-fir germinative processes.  The germination of Douglas-fir seeds in a 1% hydrogen peroxide solution occurs at a fast and hight rate. This treatment is the most effective when HO solution quickly and intimately comes in contact with the endosperm and the embryo. Even more, HO has to operate the whole germinative processes long and does not drastically overcome the inhibitory effects imposed by seed coats. It is not through a release of oxygen that HO promotes germination for an increase of the pure O external pressure does not in any way improve the results. Consequently, the beneficial effects of HO arise from a direct stimulation of the endosperm-and/or embryo-metabolism.

20794011|Morphology and cytotype of wood and grassland populations of Cardamine pratensis L. s.l. from Belgium and northern France have been studied. 20793461|During five days of summer and fall 1970, total solar radiation (300-3000 nm) and visible light (300-780 nm) were measured by means of pyranometers and photometers at the same time in a 140-year-old beech-grove (Fagus sylvatica L.), in a 56-year-old spruce plantation (Picea abies (L.) Karst.) and in the open, at the "Plateau des Tailles" in Belgian "Haute-Ardenne". On clear days, the deciduous canopy reduces incoming solar radiation in an average proportion of 91%; for the conifers, the value is 95%; the leafless deciduous canopy shuts off only 71%. Visible light is more restricted than the total solar radiation: its reduction reaches 97.5% in the beech-stand and 99% in the conifer stand. The reduction of solar radiation seems to be greater on clear weather than on cloudy or overcast conditions. The study of the relationship between solar radiation and visible light shows that the proportion of "long-wave" radiation (780-3000 nm) is greater in the forest stands, specially in the beech-grove, than in the open.

Ce fait semble suggrer que les verticilles pourraient tre impliqus dans l'absorption de la lumire et peut-tre de certaines substances nutritives dissoutes dans l'eau de mer. Les poils des verticilles montrent parfois des modifications importantes dans leur morphologie. Ils peuvent galement contenir des cystes mrs tout  fait identiques  ceux du chapeau. Des expriences de marquage avec des prcurseurs du DNA, du RNA et des protines ont montr que le cytoplasme (anucl) des verticilles isols possde une importante activit mtabolique. We have studied some aspects of the morphology and development of the whorls in Acetabularia mediterranea. The whorls, which are constituted by very long polychotomic hairs, have a surface 2-4 times larger than that of the entire stalk. This fact seems suggest that they could play a role in light absorption and perhaps in the uptake of nutritive substances dissolved in sea-water. The hairs of the whorls sometimes show important modifications in their morphology. They can contain mature cysts identical to those of the cap. Labelling experiments with some precursors of DNA, RNA and proteins have shown that the (anucleated) cytoplasm of isolated whorls is metabolically very active.

20793570|A complex of wet and marshy meadows which have settled since at least 150 years on the eutrophic alluvial deposits of the Woluwe river, near the Hof-ter-Musschen in Woluw-Saint-Lambert (Brussels, Belgium), is studied from floristic and plant sociological angle. On a limited area of about 2 ha, the complex assembles a great number (about 150) of Phanerogam species of which several have become quite rare in the Brabantine valleys, and one, Triglochin palustris, extremely rare in Belgium. It also shows quite a number of different plant communities and soil types which at present have poor possibility of replacement, not only in the greater Brussels area, but also in the whole Picardo-Brabantine district. The best individualized plant communities are related to the Glycerio-Sparganion (Apium nodiflorum-Mentha aquatica community, Glyceria maxima community), the Magnocaricion elatae (Carex acutiformis community) and the Agropyro-Rumicion (Festuca rubra-Carex disticha-Triglochin palustris community).
20792292|Reviewing, by phytogeographical districts, the different localities where Liparis Loeselii has been encountered, the author cites for each of them the litterature and the herbarium specimens. It appears clearly from this that the species is in full decrease in Belgium. Known formerly from eighteen localities, distributed into three phytogeographical districts, it survives actually only at La Panne, Oostduinkerke and Anvers left bank all located in the maritime district, and at Neerpelt in the heath district. The main reasons for its gradual disappearance are: destroying of the marshes and bogs, extension of the sea-shore cities and extensive drainage. From a phytocenological viewpoint, the author considers L. Loeselii in Belgium as a characteristic of the Caricetalia fuscae, but not as an exclusive of the Caricion Davallianae.

20793723|L'excrtion de protons par le systme radiculaire de plantules d'orge a t mesure dans diffrentes conditions exprimentales et compare  l'absorption ionique concomittante. Les diffrences constates entre traitements peuvent s'expliquer par la plus ou moins grande richesse des racines en sucres solubles. Au cours de leur catabolisme, ces sucres engendrent non seulement l'acide carbonique gnrateur de protons, mais aussi l'ATP ncessaire  l'excrtion de ces derniers. Ces diffrences dans le pouvoir d'excrtion de protons ont  leur tour des rpercussions sur l'absorption ionique et, plus directement, sur l'absorption des cations monovalents. Extrusion of protons by barley roots has been measured in different experimental conditions. Differences in proton efflux may be attributed to the variable content of the roots in soluble sugars. During their catabolic breakdown, they not only produce carbonic acid, which generates protons, but also the ATP necessary for the proton extrusion. The differences in the capacity of excreting protons are paralleled by differences in ion uptake and more specifically in absorption of monovalent cations.

Scirpus cespitosus L. subsp. germanicus (Palla) Brod. has been known for a long time in Belgium. However it was only recently that the subsp. cespitosus was reported in the Hautes Fagnes area. 20793943|La germination in vitro du pollen permet de juger ses aptitudes intrinsques  germer en dehors de toute interaction pollen-stigmate. De plus, ce test de viabilit est le meilleur et le plus fiable. Son utilisation localise rapidement une strilit mle partielle ou totale parmi une collection importante. Les essais permettent de constater le polymorphisme des grains de pollen qui germent; cette constatation est intressante pour les perspectives qu'elle laisse entrevoir pour l'amlioration des Fuchsia. This study shows that amongst the irregular pollen grains, the germination is not linked to the pore number. This observation is important for further improvement of Fuchsia.
20792795|Effects of the sodium and potassium external concentration on the chloride electrochemical potential difference of Nitella.  The chloride electrochemical potential difference, membrane potential and electrical resistance of Nitella flexilis were measured at 3C and 20C in solutions where glucuronate is progressively substituted for chloride. The predominant cation is K or Na following the experiments but the ionic strength of the medium is kept constant at 1,1 mM. Cells pretreated in Ca-free medium are used throughout the experiments. The vacuolar concentrations are 64 mM K, 43 mM Na (flame photometry) and 80 mM Cl (electrotitrimetric titration). Membrane potential and resistance are little affected by variations of chloride in the external medium but large changes occur in the chloride electrochemical potential difference. The internal chloride concentration for the whole cell calculated from the values of these parameters decreases or increases with [Cl]o in an unexpected way with the reputed low permeability of the membrane to Cl ions. A double reciprocal plot of [Cl]i and [Cl]o for both the temperatures shows that the penetration of chlorides into Nitella is easier when Na is more abundant in the external medium and that this phenomenon is linked with the metabolic energy. The discrepancy between the chloride concentration measured by titration and microelectrode and the large variations of cellular chloride activity are discussed. The more likely explanation is that the thermodynamic active chlorides are only a part of the total chloride pool. The lack of effects on membrane potential is compared with the same stability observed when vacuolar sap is exchanged with artificial solutions where chlorides ions are varied.
20792655|Radiative and thermal fluxes of the forest were studied for a clear day. Radiative balance (Q) was determined by radiation measurements with Moll-Gorczynski thermopiles and Schulze radiometers. Soil heat flux (QG), vegetation heat flux (QV) and inner air layer heat flux (QL) were measured to obtain Qi (= QG + QV + QL) which is the heat flux in the active layers of the forest. Latent heat flux (V or evapotranspiration) and sensible heat flux (K or turbulent convection) were computed according to the Bowen's ratio and the heat budget method. Daily variations of each flux are presented in fig. 1 and 2. For a whole summer clear day, Q is 308,543 cal cm min and in percents of Q, evapotranspiration is 66,6%, turbulent convection 26,5%, whereas other fluxes are smaller: heat flux in the soil is 5,1%; in the vegetation 1,2%; and in the inner air layer only 0,6%.
20792631|Throughout the year and at five different levels on the current year shoots of apple and pear trees, buds were taken and isolated with a 7 cm-piece of stem and placed in moist sand. The bacterial and fungal microflora has been studied during 1967-1968 in litters in the oak forest on, mull (Querceto-Coryletum) near Ferage (Upper Belgium). Among the bacterial flora, proteolytic, amylolytic, celluloytic and nitrogen-fixing germs were considered. The bacterial populations of litters grow up to the maximum during the first months of the year. The abundance of Nitrogen-fixing germs should lead to the assumption that they could be effective in the N increase observed by others workers in litters, more especially as they could live in symbiosis with the numerous cellulolytic germs colonizing the dead leaves. The yeasts concentration raises up to the maximum of 40.10 germs / dry gr. in the Quercus litter as well as in the Carpinus litter.

Six sites of the prave-Rochefort transect already described by Tanghe (1971) are studied to establish the relationship between the distribution of the herbaceous forest species and the characteristics of the nitrogen mineralisation.
